Case 0-Title: Marinated Flank Steak Recipe
Ingredients: ["1 1/2 pound flank steak", "1/2 c. finely minced green onions (scallions)", "1/2 c. dry red wine", "1/4 c. soy sauce", "3 tbsp. salad oil", "3 teaspoon sesame seeds", "2 teaspoon packed brown sugar", "1/4 teaspoon grnd black pepper", "1/4 teaspoon grnd ginger", "1 clove garlic, chopped"]
Directions: ["Remove tenderloin from steak.", "Score meat.", "Combine remaining ingredients and pour over meat.", "Let marinate 24 hrs.", "Preheat grill.", "Broil or possibly grill.", "Slice thinly on an angle against the grain."]
Requirement: Lupin-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Marinated Flank Steak Recipe**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 1/2 pound flank steak
- 1/2 cup finely minced green onions (scallions)
- 1/2 cup dry red wine (ensure it’s lupin-free)
- 1/4 cup tamari (gluten-free soy sauce alternative)
- 3 tablespoons avocado oil
- 3 teaspoons sesame seeds
- 2 teaspoons packed brown sugar
- 1/4 teaspoon ground black pepper
- 1/4 teaspoon ground ginger
- 1 clove garlic, chopped

**Directions:**
1. Trim any fat from the flank steak.
2. Score the meat lightly.
3. In a bowl, combine minced green onions, dry red wine, tamari, avocado oil, sesame seeds, brown sugar, black pepper, ground ginger, and chopped garlic, mixing well.
4. Place the steak in a shallow dish or a large resealable plastic bag and pour the marinade over the meat, ensuring it is well-coated.
5. Seal the container or bag and refrigerate, allowing the meat to marinate for at least 24 hours, turning occasionally.
6. Preheat a grill to medium-high heat.
7. Remove the steak from the marinade and let any excess drip off.
8. Grill or broil the flank steak to your desired doneness, typically about 5-7 minutes per side for medium-rare.
9. Remove the steak from the grill and let it rest for a few minutes.
10. Slice thinly on an angle against the grain and serve.
```

Case 1-Title: French Chicken Stew
Ingredients: ["1 tablespoon rosemary", "1 teaspoon thyme", "3 bay leaves", "1 teaspoon smoked paprika", "1 teaspoon pepper", "1/4 cup red wine", "3 cups chicken broth", "2 cups button mushrooms sliced", "2 cups mushroom mix, oyster, shiitake, baby bella, sliced", "2 medium carrots sliced diagonally", "1 onion medium, chopped", "1 red potato medium, cut in 1-inch pieces", "1 cup frozen green beans 1-inch pieces", "1/2 can black olives pitted ripe, halved", "1 handful grape tomatoes halved", "8 chicken thighs with bones and skin. 2-3 lbs", "2 stalks celery", "3 cups water"]
Directions: ["combine all ingredients in slow cooker (6 quarts). bury chicken in vegetables. don't put herbs directly on chicken (because skin is removed later)", "add enough broth and water to cover most of ingredients. liquid level rises a good amount during cooking, so careful with filling the slow cooker too much.", "turn slow cooker on low for 6-7 hours or high 3-4 hours. Note: in my newer Crock-Pot this was enough time, but in my parents' older Crock-Pot 7 hours on low was not enough (don't know how long would be good. we left the veggies a little tough).", "pull out all chicken.", "skim off fat from top with spoon", "pull off skin and remove bones from chicken. shred and return to soup."]
Requirement: Shellfish-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: French Chicken Stew**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 tablespoon rosemary
- 1 teaspoon thyme
- 3 bay leaves
- 1 teaspoon smoked paprika
- 1 teaspoon pepper
- 1/4 cup red wine (ensure wine is shellfish-free; consult producer)
- 3 cups chicken broth (ensure broth is shellfish-free)
- 2 cups button mushrooms, sliced
- 2 cups mixed mushrooms (oyster, shiitake, baby bella), sliced
- 2 medium carrots, sliced diagonally
- 1 medium onion, chopped
- 1 medium red potato, cut into 1-inch pieces
- 1 cup frozen green beans, cut into 1-inch pieces
- 1/2 can black olives, pitted ripe, halved
- 1 handful grape tomatoes, halved
- 8 chicken thighs with bones and skin, 2-3 lbs
- 2 stalks celery, chopped
- 3 cups water

**Instructions:**
1. Combine all ingredients in a 6-quart slow cooker. Bury chicken in vegetables, ensuring the chicken is well surrounded.
2. Avoid placing herbs directly on the chicken to facilitate later removal of the skin.
3. Add enough chicken broth and water to cover most ingredients. Be cautious not to overfill, as the liquid level will rise during cooking.
4. Turn the slow cooker on low for 6-7 hours or high for 3-4 hours. Cooking time may vary based on the slow cooker's model and age.
5. Once cooking is complete, pull out all chicken pieces.
6. Skim off any fat from the top of the stew with a spoon.
7. Remove the skin and bones from the chicken, shred the meat, and return it to the stew.
8. Stir well and serve warm.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

While the modified recipe seeks to address the requirement of being shellfish-free by advising to consult producers to ensure the wine and chicken broth are shellfish-free, it doesn't explicitly confirm that these products are certified shellfish-free. There is a potential risk of cross-contamination or hidden ingredients in these products that might contain shellfish residues. Ensure that the ingredients are from reliable sources and clearly labeled as shellfish-free to avoid any cross-contamination or allergy risk.

Case 2-Title: Glazed Carrots
Ingredients: ["3 to 4 carrots", "1 1/2 Tbsp. butter", "1/3 c. brown sugar", "grated lemon rind and juice"]
Directions: ["Cook 3 to 4 carrots; cut crosswise in 1-inch pieces.", "Add butter, brown sugar (packed) and grated lemon rind and juice to taste.", "Heat slow, stirring occasionally, until nicely glazed, about 15 minutes.", "Makes 2 to 3 servings."]
Requirement: Wheat-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Dish Name:** Glazed Carrots (Wheat-Free)

**Ingredients:**
- 3 to 4 carrots
- 1 1/2 Tbsp. ghee or dairy-free butter alternative
- 1/3 cup coconut sugar
- Grated zest and juice of 1 lemon

**Directions:**
1. Peel and slice 3 to 4 carrots crosswise into 1-inch pieces.
2. In a saucepan over medium heat, melt ghee or your chosen dairy-free butter alternative.
3. Add the coconut sugar, grated lemon zest, and lemon juice to the pan. Stir to combine.
4. Add the carrot pieces into the saucepan and mix well to coat them with the glaze.
5. Lower the heat and cook slowly, stirring occasionally, until the carrots are nicely glazed and tender, about 15 minutes.
6. Serve warm and enjoy. Makes 2 to 3 servings.
```

Case 3-Title: Moms Pie Dough 
Ingredients: ["4.5 Cups Flour", "1.5 Tsp Salt", "Pinch Baking Powder", "1 Tbls Sugar", "1 2/3 cup Crisco", "1 egg lightly beaten", "1 tsp vinegar", "Ice Water"]
Directions: ["Mix all dry ingredients in a bowl.", "", "Add crisco and cut in with dough cutter.", "", "Mix wet ingredients adding ice water to make 1 total cup of wet ingredients.", "", "Add wet to dry, starting with 1/2 cup of wet ingredients.", "", "Make dough and chill"]
Requirement: Celery-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Moms Pie Dough**

**Ingredients:**
- 4.5 Cups All-Purpose Flour
- 1.5 Tsp Salt
- Pinch Baking Powder
- 1 Tbls Sugar
- 1 2/3 Cup Unsalted Butter, chilled and diced
- 1 Egg, lightly beaten
- 1 Tsp White Vinegar
- Ice Water

**Instructions:**
1. In a large bowl, mix together the flour, salt, baking powder, and sugar.
2. Add the chilled, diced unsalted butter to the dry ingredients and work it in using a pastry cutter until the mixture resembles coarse crumbs.
3. In a separate measuring cup or small bowl, combine the beaten egg and white vinegar. Add enough ice water to make a total of 1 cup of liquid.
4. Gradually add the wet ingredients to the dry ingredients, starting with 1/2 cup, and mix gently just until the dough starts to come together. Avoid over-mixing.
5. Form the dough into a ball and wrap it in plastic wrap. Chill it in the refrigerator for at least 1 hour before using.
```

Case 4-Title: Pretzel Salad Or Dessert
Ingredients: ["2 c. crushed small thin pretzels (sticks)", "3/4 c. margarine"]
Directions: ["Mix and press in baking pan, approximately 13 x 9-inch. Bake 8 minutes at 400\u00b0. Cool."]
Requirement: Sesame-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
### Modified Recipe: Pretzel Salad or Dessert

#### Ingredients
- 2 cups crushed small thin pretzels (ensure they are sesame-free)
- 3/4 cup unsalted butter or a non-dairy margarine alternative (ensure it is sesame-free)

#### Directions
1. Preheat your oven to 400°F (200°C).
2. In a medium-sized bowl, mix the crushed sesame-free pretzels with the unsalted butter or sesame-free non-dairy margarine until well combined.
3. Press the pretzel mixture evenly into the bottom of a 13 x 9-inch baking pan to form a crust.
4. Bake the crust in the preheated oven for 8 minutes.
5. Remove from the oven and allow it to cool completely before using in your preferred salad or dessert recipe.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- Ensure that both the pretzels and the non-dairy margarine alternative are certified sesame-free to avoid cross-contamination or cross-reactivity risks. Even if the ingredient list does not include sesame, it is crucial that the product packaging confirms it is manufactured in a sesame-free facility.

Case 5-Title: Citrus Syrup
Ingredients: ["3/4 cup sugar", "1/2 cup fresh orange juice", "1/2 cup fresh lemon juice"]
Directions: ["In a 1 1/2-quart saucepan stir together sugar and juices and simmer, stirring occasionally, 5 minutes, or until sugar is dissolved and syrup is slightly thickened.", "Cool syrup.", "Syrup may be made 3 days ahead and chilled, covered.", "Makes about 1 1/4 cups."]
Requirement: Tree nut-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Citrus Syrup**

**Ingredients:**
- 3/4 cup sugar (certified tree nut-free)
- 1/2 cup fresh orange juice (certified tree nut-free)
- 1/2 cup fresh lemon juice (certified tree nut-free)

**Instructions:**
1. Ensure all work surfaces, utensils, and cooking equipment are thoroughly cleaned to avoid any cross-contamination with tree nuts.
2. In a 1 1/2-quart saucepan, stir together sugar, orange juice, and lemon juice.
3. Simmer the mixture over medium heat, stirring occasionally, for about 5 minutes or until the sugar is fully dissolved and the syrup is slightly thickened.
4. Remove the syrup from heat and allow it to cool.
5. Transfer the cooled syrup to a clean, nut-free container and cover it. The syrup can be made up to 3 days ahead and should be stored in the refrigerator.
6. Makes about 1 1/4 cups of citrus syrup.
```

Case 6-Title: Cranberry And Candied Orange Chutney 
Ingredients: ["1 large navel orange with skin", "7 cups water, divided", "1/2 cup sugar", "2 cinnamon sticks, divided", "1/4 cup (packed) golden brown sugar", "1 tablespoon dark rum", "2 teaspoons apple cider vinegar", "1/8 teaspoon ground allspice", "1/2 cup fresh or frozen cranberries"]
Directions: ["Cut orange into 1/4-inch-thick rounds; cut rounds into 1/4-inch cubes. Place in heavy medium saucepan; add 3 cups water. Bring to boil. Reduce heat and simmer 10 minutes. Drain, rinse, and drain well. Boil again with 3 cups water; rinse and drain.", "Return orange cubes to same pan. Add 3/4 cup water, 1/2 cup sugar, and 1 cinnamon stick. Bring to boil, stirring until sugar dissolves. Boil gently until all liquid evaporates, about 30 minutes.", "Bring brown sugar, rum, vinegar, allspice, 1/4 cup water, and 1 cinnamon stick to boil in saucepan. Mix in cranberries. Cook until thick syrup forms, stirring occasionally, about 10 minutes. Mix in orange; cook 1 minute. Transfer chutney to small bowl; cool. (Can be made 2 days ahead. Cover; chill.)"]
Requirement: Peanut-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Cranberry And Candied Orange Chutney**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 large navel orange with skin
- 7 cups water, divided
- 1/2 cup granulated sugar
- 2 cinnamon sticks, divided
- 1/4 cup (packed) golden brown sugar
- 1 tablespoon dark rum (ensure it's peanut-free or use a certified gluten-free variety)
- 2 teaspoons apple cider vinegar
- 1/8 teaspoon ground allspice
- 1/2 cup fresh or frozen cranberries

**Directions:**
1. Cut the orange into 1/4-inch-thick rounds; then cut the rounds into 1/4-inch cubes.
2. Place the cubed oranges in a heavy medium saucepan and add 3 cups water. Bring to a boil. Reduce the heat and simmer for 10 minutes. Drain, rinse with fresh water, and drain well. Repeat the process by boiling with another 3 cups water, rinse, and then drain.
3. Return the orange cubes to the same pan. Add 3/4 cup water, 1/2 cup granulated sugar, and 1 cinnamon stick. Bring to a boil, stirring until the sugar dissolves. Boil gently until all the liquid evaporates, approximately 30 minutes.
4. Meanwhile, in another saucepan, bring the brown sugar, dark rum (ensured peanut-free), apple cider vinegar, allspice, 1/4 cup water, and the other cinnamon stick to a boil.
5. Mix in the cranberries and cook until a thick syrup forms, stirring occasionally, about 10 minutes.
6. Mix the candied orange into the cranberry mixture and cook for an additional 1 minute.
7. Transfer the chutney to a small bowl and allow it to cool. This dish can be made up to 2 days ahead; cover and chill if preparing in advance.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

The modified recipe attempts to meet the peanut-free requirement by specifying the use of peanut-free or certified gluten-free dark rum. However, it is essential to ensure all other ingredients are also verified for potential cross-contamination with peanuts, including sugar and cinnamon sticks. Without explicit certification or assurance for these ingredients, caution is advised. Additionally, if any utensils or surfaces were used previously for peanut-containing dishes, they must be thoroughly cleaned to avoid cross-contamination risks. If any ingredient that cannot be certified nut-free is used, it is better to avoid using those until confirmation.

Case 7-Title: Tau Kua He Ci Medan'S Favourite Food 
Ingredients: ["1 slices Gravy ingredients (A) - onion", "3 cloves Gravy ingredients (A) - cloves garlic", "300 grams Gravy ingredients (A) - very ripe tomatoes (chopped)", "300 grams Gravy ingredients (A) - pineappled (chopped)", "6 tablespoons Gravy ingredients (A) - tomato sauce ( i use Del Monte)", "3 tablespoons Gravy ingredients (A) - sugar ( to taste)", "1 tablespoon Gravy ingredients (A) - salt & pepper", "3 liters Gravy ingredients (A) - water", "200 grams Gravy ingredients (B) - pineappled (chopped)", "3 tablespoons Gravy ingredients (B) - corn starch to dissolve in water"]
Directions: ["The condiments:", "- Large prawns, fried in batter", "- Small blue swimming crab, fried in batter", "- small - medium size prawn, made into crackers", "- 1 bunch of morning glory, boil until ready", "- 200 gr bean sprout, blanched", "- make birds eye chilli sauce", "The Gravy :", "- Bring water to a boil, put all ingredients for gravy and continue to cooke for 10 minutes, simmer for another 1 hour or until the tomato is softened or the water has reduced to 2 - 2.5 L", "- Put the tomato stock back in the pot, add in the dissolved corn starch, mix well and bring back to a boil, the gravy now should thickened. If you prefer the gravy slightly runny use 2 tbsp of corn starch but if you wish thicker use 3 tbsp.", "- The gravy is now ready to use"]
Requirement: Lupin-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
### Modified Recipe for Tau Kua He Ci Medan's Favourite Food

#### Ingredients:
- **Gravy Ingredients (A):**
  - 1 slice onion
  - 3 cloves garlic
  - 300 grams very ripe tomatoes, chopped
  - 300 grams pineapple, chopped
  - 6 tablespoons tomato sauce (ensure lupin-free brand)
  - 3 tablespoons sugar, or to taste
  - 1 tablespoon salt & pepper, to taste
  - 3 liters water

- **Gravy Ingredients (B):**
  - 200 grams pineapple, chopped
  - 3 tablespoons cornstarch, dissolved in water

- **Condiments:**
  - Large prawns, fried in a batter (ensure batter is lupin-free)
  - Small blue swimming crab, fried in a batter (ensure batter is lupin-free)
  - Small to medium-sized prawn crackers (ensure lupin-free)
  - 1 bunch of morning glory, boiled until ready
  - 200 grams bean sprouts, blanched
  - Birds eye chili sauce (ensure lupin-free)

#### Instructions:
1. **The Gravy:**
   - In a large pot, bring the water to a boil.
   - Add all the Gravy Ingredients (A) and cook for 10 minutes.
   - Reduce the heat and simmer for another 1 hour, or until the tomatoes are softened and the liquid has reduced to 2 - 2.5 liters.
   - Stir in the Gravy Ingredients (B) by adding the dissolved cornstarch into the tomato stock.
   - Mix well and bring the gravy back to a boil. Adjust the thickness by using 2 tablespoons of cornstarch for a runnier gravy or 3 tablespoons for a thicker consistency.
   - The gravy is now ready to be used.

2. **Serving:**
   - Serve the gravy hot with the prepared condiments: fried prawns, fried crab, lupin-free prawn crackers, boiled morning glory, blanched bean sprouts, and birds eye chili sauce.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

While the modified recipe aims to cater to a lupin-free requirement by identifying ingredients that need to be lupin-free (tomato sauce, batter for prawns and crab, prawn crackers, and chili sauce), the recipe relies heavily on ensuring that these substitutions are indeed certified lupin-free. However, without explicit certification mentioned, there's a potential risk of cross-contamination or mislabeling which requires caution. Each of these ingredients should be verified with a certified lupin-free label to ensure safety.

Case 8-Title: Jamaica Barbecue Sauce
Ingredients: ["1 1/2 c. cider vinegar", "4 tsp. lemon juice", "3 tsp. Worcestershire sauce", "2 tsp. brown sugar", "1 Tbsp. prepared mustard", "3/4 tsp. salt", "1/2 tsp. meat tenderizer", "1 c. tomato catsup", "1 Tbsp. liquid smoke", "1 tsp. garlic powder", "1 tsp. cayenne pepper", "1/2 tomato puree"]
Directions: ["Mix ingredients well.", "Pour into jar.", "Keep in refrigerator until ready to use.", "Makes 1 3/4 pints."]
Requirement: Mustard-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Dish Name:** Jamaica Barbecue Sauce (Mustard-Free)

**Ingredients:**
- 1 1/2 cups apple cider vinegar
- 4 tsp. lemon juice
- 3 tsp. Worcestershire sauce (ensure gluten-free if needed)
- 2 tsp. brown sugar
- 1 Tbsp. horseradish (prepared)
- 3/4 tsp. salt
- 1/2 tsp. meat tenderizer (ensure gluten-free if needed)
- 1 cup tomato ketchup (ensure gluten-free if needed)
- 1 Tbsp. liquid smoke
- 1 tsp. garlic powder
- 1 tsp. cayenne pepper
- 1/2 cup tomato puree

**Directions:**
1. Combine all ingredients in a large mixing bowl.
2. Whisk together until all ingredients are thoroughly mixed and the sauce is smooth.
3. Transfer the sauce into a clean jar with a tight-fitting lid.
4. Store in the refrigerator until ready to use.
5. Makes approximately 1 3/4 pints.
```

Case 9-Title: Dill Dip
Ingredients: ["2/3 c. sour cream", "2/3 c. Hellmann's mayo", "1 Tbsp. parsley flakes", "1 Tbsp. dried onion flakes", "1 Tbsp. Worcestershire sauce", "1 tsp. Accent", "1 tsp. season salt", "1 tsp. dill weed"]
Directions: ["Mix all ingredients together and chill overnight. Great with fresh vegetables."]
Requirement: Soy-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Soy-Free Dill Dip**

**Ingredients:**
- 2/3 cup full-fat Greek yogurt
- 2/3 cup soy-free mayonnaise (ensure it is labeled soy-free)
- 1 tablespoon parsley flakes
- 1 tablespoon dried onion flakes
- 1 tablespoon coconut aminos (as a substitute for Worcestershire sauce)
- 1 teaspoon celery salt (as a substitute for Accent)
- 1 teaspoon season salt
- 1 teaspoon dill weed

**Directions:**
1. In a medium-sized bowl, combine the Greek yogurt and soy-free mayonnaise until smooth.
2. Stir in the parsley flakes, dried onion flakes, coconut aminos, celery salt, season salt, and dill weed until well blended.
3. Cover and refrigerate the dip overnight to allow flavors to meld.
4. Serve chilled with fresh vegetables.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- Ensure that the substitute for mayonnaise is explicitly labeled as "soy-free" to avoid cross-contamination risks.
- Confirm that the coconut aminos used as a substitute for Worcestershire sauce is certified soy-free, as some products might contain soy or be processed in facilities that handle soy.
- Validate any additional flavorings or seasoning mixes (such as celery salt or seasoned salt) to ensure they do not contain soy derivatives and are also processed in soy-free environments, to maintain the soy-free requirement.

Case 10-Title: Crab, Grapefruit And Watercress Salad
Ingredients: ["3 tablespoons champagne vinegar", "3 tablespoons honey", "2 tablespoons chopped sweet onion", "1 teaspoon Dijon mustard", "1/2 teaspoon sea salt", "1/2 cup canola oil", "1 tablespoon poppy seeds", "2 cans (6-1/2 ounces each) jumbo lump crabmeat, drained {Maria: the flavor of jumbo lump crabmeat is much better than plain old lump crabmeat plus it's more tender, so please be sure to get jumbo. thx!}", "6 cups watercress", "2-1/2 cups fresh grapefruit segments", "12 cherry tomatoes, halved", "1 medium ripe avocado, peeled, pitted and sliced", "1-1/2 teaspoons white grapefruit juice"]
Directions: ["Process first five ingredients in a blender or food processor until smooth. While processing, gradually add oil in a steady stream until dressing thickens. Pour into a serving bowl; stir in poppy seeds.", "Transfer 1/4 cup salad dressing to a small bowl. Toss with crab. Add remaining ingredients to serving bowl; gently toss until combined. Top with crab mixture."]
Requirement: Celery-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Dish Name:** Crab, Grapefruit And Watercress Salad (Celery-Free Version)

**Ingredients:**
- 3 tablespoons champagne vinegar
- 3 tablespoons honey
- 2 tablespoons chopped sweet onion
- 1 teaspoon Dijon mustard (ensure it's celery-free; check labels)
- 1/2 teaspoon sea salt
- 1/2 cup grapeseed oil (ensure it's celery-free; check labels)
- 1 tablespoon poppy seeds
- 2 cans (6-1/2 ounces each) jumbo lump crabmeat, drained (ensure no cross-contamination with celery)
- 6 cups watercress
- 2-1/2 cups fresh grapefruit segments
- 12 cherry tomatoes, halved
- 1 medium ripe avocado, peeled, pitted, and sliced
- 1-1/2 teaspoons white grapefruit juice

**Instructions:**
1. **Prepare Dressing**: In a blender or food processor, combine champagne vinegar, honey, chopped sweet onion, Dijon mustard, and sea salt. Blend until smooth.
2. **Incorporate Oil**: While the blender is running, gradually add the grapeseed oil in a steady stream until the dressing thickens. Pour the dressing into a serving bowl and stir in poppy seeds.
3. **Toss Crab**: Transfer 1/4 cup of the prepared salad dressing to a small bowl. Toss the crabmeat in the dressing, ensuring thorough coating.
4. **Assemble Salad**: In a large serving bowl, combine watercress, grapefruit segments, cherry tomatoes, and sliced avocado. Gently toss with the remaining dressing until well coated.
5. **Final Assembly**: Top the salad with the dressed crab mixture. Serve immediately.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

• Ingredient Safety: The modified recipe takes precautions to ensure that mustard, grapeseed oil, and crabmeat are certified celery-free and not cross-contaminated with celery. However, the instruction relies on the assurance that labels are checked for celery-free certification. This approach presents a potential risk if not explicitly confirmed. Additionally, cross-contamination, especially in pre-packaged products like crabmeat, is a concern. Make sure all products are certified celery-free, especially in a regulated production facility.

• Requirement Fulfillment: While the substitutions appear to be celery-free, they'd need confirmed certifications to ensure that cross-contamination is not a risk.

Please ensure that all ingredients have been explicitly confirmed as celery-free with appropriate certification to ensure safety.

Case 11-Title: Sloppy Joe Grilled Cheese
Ingredients: ["1 pound ground beef", "1/4 cup chopped onion", "2 tablespoons prepared mustard depending on your tastebuds", "1/2 cup ketchup", "1/4 cup brown sugar", "1/2 tablespoon worcestershire sauce", "12 slices Texas toast bread", "6 tablespoons butter softened", "4 cups shredded cheese or more if you need it"]
Directions: ["Read full directions at 5boysbaker.com"]
Requirement: Sulfite-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Sulfite-Free Sloppy Joe Grilled Cheese**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 pound ground beef, grass-fed if possible
- 1/4 cup chopped onion
- 2 tablespoons whole grain mustard (ensure sulfite-free)
- 1/2 cup organic tomato paste
- 1/4 cup coconut sugar or packed maple sugar
- 1/2 tablespoon coconut aminos (alternative to Worcestershire sauce)
- 12 slices sulfite-free sourdough bread
- 6 tablespoons unsalted butter, softened
- 4 cups shredded cheddar cheese, dairy or plant-based (ensure sulfite-free)

**Directions:**
1. In a skillet over medium heat, cook ground beef and onion until the beef is browned and the onion is soft. Drain excess fat if needed.
2. Stir in whole grain mustard, tomato paste, coconut sugar, and coconut aminos. Cook for 5-7 minutes until the mixture thickens slightly. Set aside.
3. Butter one side of each slice of sourdough bread.
4. Preheat a non-stick skillet or griddle over medium heat.
5. Place half of the slices of bread butter-side down onto the skillet. Top each with a generous amount of the beef mixture and then with shredded cheese.
6. Top with the remaining slices of bread, butter-side up.
7. Grill each sandwich for about 3-4 minutes on each side, or until the bread is golden brown and the cheese has melted.
8. Serve immediately and enjoy your sulfite-free Sloppy Joe Grilled Cheese!

```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- **Ingredient Safety**: While the modified recipe states to use sulfite-free ingredients, there is potential for cross-contamination or residual sulfites if the products used are not explicitly labeled as sulfite-free. Ensure that mustard, tomato paste, coconut sugar, coconut aminos, sourdough bread, and shredded cheddar cheese are certified sulfite-free to fully comply with the requirement.

- **Requirement Fulfillment**: The common culprits for sulfites, such as Worcestershire sauce and certain sugars, have been substituted. However, general vigilance is required in sourcing all ingredients to ensure the sulfite-free claim is met without ambiguity.

Case 12-Title: Strawberry Tart
Ingredients: ["1 pie shell Graham Cracker", "2 cups low fat milk", "1 package sugar free vanilla instant pudding mix", "1 teaspoon orange rind grated freshly", "2 cups strawberries cleaned &", "berries Hauled, other, maybe substituted"]
Directions: ["Use an 8- or 9-inch tart pan with removeable bottom.", "Firmly pat gramham cracker pie shell into tart pan.", "Set aside. Blend milk with instant pudding mix in deep bowl using a whisk or an electric mixer. Continue mixing at low speed for 1 minute or until pudding is dissolved. Add grated orange rind. Let stand for 5 minutes and pour into pie shell. Let stand for 15 minutes or until set. Arrange strawberries or other berries decoratively over pudding shortly before This recipe is suitable for occasional use. Use unsalted margarine in pie shell."]
Requirement: Lupin-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Strawberry Tart Recipe**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 pie shell made from nut-based or gluten-free flour (ensure lupin-free)
- 2 cups almond milk or coconut milk
- 1 package vanilla instant pudding mix (ensure it is lupin-free and dairy-free)
- 1 teaspoon freshly grated orange rind
- 2 cups strawberries, cleaned and hulled (or a mix of other berries)

**Directions:**
1. Preheat the oven to 350°F (175°C). Lightly grease an 8- or 9-inch tart pan with a removable bottom.
2. Firmly pat the nut-based or gluten-free pie shell into the tart pan, pressing it evenly across the bottom and up the sides.
3. Place the pan on a baking sheet and bake the shell for 8-10 minutes, or until lightly golden. Remove from the oven and let it cool completely.
4. In a deep bowl, blend almond milk or coconut milk with the vanilla instant pudding mix using a whisk or an electric mixer on low speed for 1 minute or until the pudding is dissolved and the mixture thickens. Stir in the grated orange rind.
5. Pour the pudding mixture into the cooled pie shell and spread it evenly.
6. Let the filled shell stand for about 15 minutes at room temperature, or until the pudding is set.
7. Shortly before serving, arrange the strawberries or other berries decoratively over the set pudding.
8. Serve chilled. Store any leftovers in the refrigerator.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- **Ingredient Safety**: The nut-based or gluten-free pie shell could potentially contain nuts that may be cross-contaminated with lupins. Ensure that ingredients are explicitly certified lupin-free, especially the nut-based flour. If there is any risk of cross-contamination with lupin, the recipe would not be completely lupin-free.

- **Requirement Fulfillment**: The vanilla instant pudding mix must also be checked to ensure it is certified lupin-free. Some processed ingredients could have unforeseen contamination risks.

Case 16-Title: Portzelky (New Year'S Cookies)
Ingredients: ["1 teaspoon sugar", "1/2 cup lukewarm water", "2 teaspoons active dry yeast", "1/2 cup milk", "1/2 cup water", "1/2 tablespoon salt", "1 tablespoon sugar", "2 teaspoons baking powder", "2 cups raisins (or as many as you would like)", "3 egg yolks", "3 egg whites, beaten", "3 cups flour", "oil (for deep frying)"]
Directions: ["Dissolve sugar in lukewarm water in a small bowl. Sprinkle with yeast and let stand.", "Combine milk, water, salt, sugar, baking powder, and raisins in a large bowl or in the bowl of a stand mixer.", "Beat in egg yolks and yeast.", "Stir in flour to make a heavy (rather stiff) batter.", "Fold in egg whites.", "Cover and set in a warm place until well risen (at least double in bulk). This should take about 2 hours. The end result is a fairly sticky dough.", "Drop by tablespoonfuls into hot oil (375F) and fry until golden brown."]
Requirement: Gluten-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Dish Name:** Gluten-Free Portzelky (New Year's Cookies)

**Ingredients:**
- 1 teaspoon sugar
- 1/2 cup lukewarm water
- 2 teaspoons active dry yeast
- 1/2 cup almond milk (or any preferred non-dairy milk)
- 1/2 cup water
- 1/2 tablespoon salt
- 1 tablespoon sugar
- 2 teaspoons gluten-free baking powder
- 2 cups raisins (or as many as you would like)
- 3 egg yolks
- 3 egg whites, beaten until stiff
- 1 1/2 cups gluten-free all-purpose flour blend
- 1/2 cup almond flour
- Oil for deep frying (use a high smoke point oil like canola or avocado oil)

**Directions:**
1. Dissolve 1 teaspoon sugar in lukewarm water in a small bowl. Sprinkle with yeast and let stand until frothy.
2. In a large bowl or the bowl of a stand mixer, combine almond milk, water, salt, 1 tablespoon sugar, gluten-free baking powder, and raisins.
3. Beat in the egg yolks and the yeast mixture.
4. Mix in gluten-free all-purpose flour and almond flour to make a heavy (rather stiff) batter.
5. Gently fold in the beaten egg whites until well incorporated.
6. Cover the bowl and set it in a warm place to rise until the dough has doubled in bulk, about 2 hours. The result should be a fairly sticky dough.
7. Heat oil in a deep fryer or large pot to 375°F (190°C).
8. Drop the dough by tablespoonfuls into the hot oil and fry until golden brown on all sides.
9. Remove the cookies with a slotted spoon and drain on paper towels before serving.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- **Edibility and Nutritional Sense**: The modified recipe utilizes almond flour and a gluten-free all-purpose flour blend to replace regular flour. While this substitution generally works, it may alter the texture and flavor of the cookies. Ensure the gluten-free flour blend used is suitable for deep-frying applications to maintain texture and structure.
  
- **Ingredient Safety**: Almond milk and almond flour introduce the risk of nut allergies and potential cross-contamination. Although the recipe aims to be gluten-free, it increases the risk for those with nut allergies. Ensure all ingredients, including the non-dairy milk substitute, are certified gluten-free to prevent cross-contamination risks.

- **Requirement Fulfillment**: The primary requirement for the recipe is to be gluten-free. Assuming the gluten-free all-purpose flour blend and other ingredients are certified gluten-free, this requirement should be met.

- **Cooking Steps**: The steps are logical and feasible with the provided gluten-free ingredients. Ensure the batter reaches the appropriate consistency to avoid issues while frying.

In summary, the gluten-free requirement seems to be fulfilled, but careful attention should be given to the safety regarding nut allergies and cross-contamination.

Case 17-Title: Frozen Fruit Medley
Ingredients: ["1 (17 ounce) can apricots or (17 ounce) can peaches", "1 (20 ounce) can unsweetend crushed pineapple", "1 cup juice or 1 cup syrup, drained from canned fruit", "1/2 cup sugar", "2 cups strawberries (or 16 oz pkg whole frozen unsweetened berries paritally thawed and separated)", "3 bananas, sliced", "1 (6 ounce) can frozen orange juice concentrate", "2 tablespoons lemon juice"]
Directions: ["Drain canned fruits, reserving 1 cup combined syrup.", "Cook syrup and sugar over medium heat about 5 minutes, stirring until sugar dissolves.", "In a large bowl, mix all ingredients including syrup together.", "Using about 2 cups at a time, place mixture in blender.", "Cover and puree until smooth but slightly chunky.", "Pour into another large bowl.", "Repeat until all fruit is processed.", "When all is blended, stir together in the large bowl.", "Line 30 muffin cups with paper liners.", "Ladle fruit into paper cups.", "Freeze until solid.", "When frozen, turn over muffin tins and punch out cups with your thumbs.", "Place cups in freezer bags and store in freezer.", "Remove from freezer 20 minutes before serving to use as a salad or dessert, or eat frozen."]
Requirement: Egg-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Frozen Fruit Medley**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 (17 ounce) can apricots or peaches in 100% fruit juice
- 1 (20 ounce) can unsweetened crushed pineapple
- 1 cup juice, drained from canned fruit
- 1/4 cup maple syrup (or another suitable sweetener)
- 2 cups strawberries (or 16 oz pkg whole frozen unsweetened berries, partially thawed and separated)
- 3 bananas, sliced
- 1 (6 ounce) can frozen orange juice concentrate
- 2 tablespoons fresh lemon juice

**Directions:**
1. Drain the canned fruits, reserving 1 cup of combined fruit juice.
2. In a small saucepan, combine the reserved fruit juice and maple syrup. Cook over medium heat for about 5 minutes, stirring until well combined.
3. In a large bowl, mix all the fruits, orange juice concentrate, lemon juice, and the maple syrup mixture together.
4. Working in batches, place about 2 cups of the fruit mixture in a blender.
5. Cover and puree until smooth but slightly chunky.
6. Transfer the blended mixture to another large bowl. Repeat until all fruit is processed.
7. Once all the fruit has been blended, stir the mixture together in the large bowl.
8. Line 30 muffin cups with paper liners.
9. Ladle the fruit mixture into the paper-lined muffin cups.
10. Freeze until solid.
11. Once frozen, remove the muffin tins from the freezer and push from the bottom to pop out the frozen fruit cups.
12. Place the cups in freezer bags and store in the freezer.
13. For serving, remove from the freezer 20 minutes before use to enjoy as a salad or dessert, or consume directly as a frozen treat.
```

Case 18-Title: Banana Slush
Ingredients: ["3 cups Water", "2 cups Sugar", "177 milliliters Orange Juice Concentrate", "6 Tablespoons Lemon Juice", "6 whole Ripe Bananas", "1.36 liters Pineapple Juice", "2 bottles (2-liter Size) Lemon-Line Soda"]
Directions: ["Note: The slush mixture makes approximately 1 gallon. Once you mix it with soda, it will make a total of 2 gallons.", "Start by preparing 2 half-gallon containers that you will use for freezing. You can mix everything in a huge bowl if you have one or divide it as you go, and mix it individually in your containers.", "Microwave water until very warm. Pour in blender, add sugar and blend until sugar is dissolved. Add orange juice concentrate and lemon juice to blender and blend on high until totally smooth. Add contents of blender to the huge mixing bowl.", "Add half the bananas and half of the pineapple juice to the blender. Blend on high until smooth. Add contents of the blender to the mixing bowl.", "Add remaining bananas and pineapple juice to the blender. Blend until smooth. Add to mixing bowl.", "Mix juices until totally combined. Pour into freezing containers and close them tightly. Freeze about 24 hours until frozen solid.", "Remove 1/2 gallon frozen slush mixture 1 hour before you are serving it. After letting it thaw on the counter for 1 hour, use a table knife to cut it in two directions. I normally cut it into about 1/2 inch sections. Add 2 liters of soda to a gallon pitcher. Spoon slush mixture into pitcher. Stir gently to combine. Adding the soda first reduces the amount of foam in your pitcher.", "Repeat previous step if you are making the whole recipe at once. This can also be made in a 2-gallon punch bowl instead of 2 gallon-sized pitchers."]
Requirement: Peanut-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Banana Slush (Peanut-Free)**

**Ingredients:**
- 3 cups Water
- 2 cups Sugar
- 177 milliliters Orange Juice Concentrate
- 6 Tablespoons Lemon Juice
- 6 whole Ripe Bananas
- 1.36 liters Pineapple Juice
- 2 bottles (2-liter Size) Lemon-Lime Soda (check for peanut-free labeling)

**Directions:**
1. Prepare 2 half-gallon freezer-safe containers. For mixing, either use a large bowl or mix individually in containers.
2. Microwave the water until very warm. Pour it into a blender, add the sugar, and blend until the sugar dissolves completely.
3. Add the orange juice concentrate and lemon juice to the blender. Blend on high until smooth. Pour contents into a large mixing bowl.
4. Add half of the bananas and half of the pineapple juice to the blender. Blend on high until smooth. Pour the mixture into the large mixing bowl.
5. Add the remaining bananas and pineapple juice to the blender. Blend until smooth and add to the mixing bowl.
6. Combine the mixtures thoroughly. Pour the mixture into the prepared freezer containers and seal them tightly. Freeze for about 24 hours until solid.
7. An hour before serving, remove 1/2 gallon of the frozen slush from the freezer. Let it thaw for about 1 hour, then use a table knife to cut the slush into roughly 1/2 inch sections.
8. Pour 2 liters of lemon-lime soda into a gallon pitcher. Add the slush mixture by spooning it into the pitcher. Stir gently to combine, reducing foam.
9. Repeat step 8 for the remaining mixture if serving the entire recipe or use a 2-gallon punch bowl for full batches.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

The modified recipe attempts to meet the peanut-free requirement by advising to check the lemon-lime soda for peanut-free labeling. However, without explicit certification or labeling details for all ingredients, especially for processed items like lemon-lime soda, there is a potential risk of cross-contamination. It is crucial to verify that all ingredients used are certified peanut-free to ensure safety for individuals with peanut allergies.

Case 20-Title: Caramel Snappers

Directions: ["To toast pecan halves, spread nuts in a single layer in a shallow baking pan.", "Toast the nuts in a 350\u00b0 oven about 10 minutes, stirring occasionally."]
Requirement: Egg-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Dish Name:** Caramel Snappers (Egg-Free)

**Modified Recipe:**

Ingredients:
- 90 pecan halves (about 1 1/2 cups)
- 1/2 (14 oz.) pkg. dairy-free and egg-free vanilla caramels (about 25)
- 1 Tbsp. water
- 1/2 cup egg-free dark chocolate pieces

**Instructions:**

1. Preheat the oven to 350°F (175°C).

2. Spread the pecan halves in a single layer on a shallow baking pan.

3. Toast the pecans in the preheated oven for about 10 minutes, stirring occasionally, until they are aromatic and lightly browned.

4. While the pecans are toasting, unwrap the dairy-free and egg-free vanilla caramels and place them in a microwave-safe bowl.

5. Add 1 tablespoon of water to the caramels and microwave on medium power in 30-second intervals, stirring after each interval, until the caramels are fully melted and smooth.

6. Arrange the toasted pecans in clusters of three on a baking sheet lined with parchment paper.

7. Drizzle or spoon the melted caramel over each pecan cluster, ensuring each pecan gets a bit of caramel.

8. Melt the egg-free dark chocolate pieces in a separate microwave-safe bowl. Microwave on medium power in 30-second intervals, stirring after each interval, until the chocolate is fully melted and smooth.

9. Drizzle or spoon the melted chocolate over the caramel-topped pecan clusters.

10. Let the Caramel Snappers sit at room temperature or refrigerate them until the caramel and chocolate are set.

11. Once set, store the Caramel Snappers in an airtight container.

Note: Always verify all ingredients, particularly caramels and chocolate, for certification that they are egg-free and produced in environments free from cross-contamination with eggs.
```

```markdown
**Pine Nut Cookie Cups (Sulfite-Free Version)**

**Ingredients:**
- Unscented coconut oil spray (as a sulfite-free alternative to nonstick spray)
- 1/2 cup pine nuts, toasted
- 1/2 cup granulated sugar
- 1/4 cup whole grain spelt flour (sulfite-free and for added nutrition)
- 5 tablespoons unsalted butter, melted (ensure it is sulfite-free)
- 2 large egg whites, beaten to blend
- 1/2 teaspoon pure vanilla extract (check label for sulfite-free)
- 1/3 cup pine nuts, untoasted

**Directions:**
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C).
2. Spray a large baking sheet with unscented coconut oil spray.
3. In a food processor, finely grind 1/2 cup toasted pine nuts with the sugar and spelt flour.
4. Transfer the mixture to a bowl.
5. Mix in the melted butter, egg whites, and vanilla extract.
6. For each cookie, spoon 1 tablespoon of batter onto the prepared baking sheet, spacing them 4 inches apart.
7. Using a knife, spread each portion into a 4-inch round.
8. Sprinkle each round with 1 teaspoon of untoasted pine nuts.
9. Bake the cookies until golden around the edges, about 10 minutes.
10. Working quickly, run a thin metal spatula around the edges of the cookies to loosen them.
11. Drape each cookie over an inverted 3/4-cup custard cup, molding and crimping the sides of the cookie to shape (cookie cups will be shallow).
12. Transfer cookies to a rack to cool.
13. Repeat with remaining batter and untoasted pine nuts, re-spraying the baking sheet with coconut oil spray between batches.
14. Allow to cool completely before use.
15. (Can be prepared 3 days ahead. Store at room temperature in an airtight container.)
```

I found the cookies took about 10 minutes to bake, but I would check after 9 to see if they are done. Let cool, or enjoy while they are warm and fuzzy."]

The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
### Modified Recipe: Gluten-Free Chocolate Oinks

**Ingredients:**
- 2 1/4 cups gluten-free all-purpose flour blend (ensure it contains xanthan gum or add 1/2 teaspoon)
- 1 teaspoon baking soda
- 1 teaspoon salt
- 1 cup (2 sticks) unsalted butter
- 3/4 cup white granulated sugar
- 3/4 cup light brown sugar, packed
- 1 1/4 teaspoons pure vanilla extract
- 2 large eggs
- 12 ounces gluten-free semi-sweet chocolate chips
- 1 package thick-cut bacon (at least 11 slices), gluten-free certified
- 1/8 cup additional light brown sugar, approximately

**Directions:**
1. Preheat the oven to 350 degrees Fahrenheit. Arrange bacon slices on a baking pan lined with parchment paper or a Silpat. Sprinkle with brown sugar. Bake for about 12 minutes, flip the slices, then bake for another 12 minutes until nice and brown. Allow bacon to cool on a rack or paper towels. Break into pieces and press between more paper towels to remove excess grease.

2. Increase the oven temperature to 375 degrees Fahrenheit. In a large mixing bowl, beat together the butter, white sugar, brown sugar, and vanilla extract until light and fluffy. Mix in the eggs one at a time, making sure each is fully incorporated before adding the next.

3. In a separate bowl, whisk together the gluten-free flour blend, baking soda, and salt. Gradually add the dry mixture to the wet ingredients, mixing until well combined.

4. Stir in the gluten-free chocolate chips and crumbled bacon pieces until evenly distributed throughout the dough.

5. Drop 1 tablespoon-sized balls of dough onto a cookie sheet lined with a Silpat or greased parchment paper.

6. Bake in the preheated oven for about 10 minutes, checking at 9 minutes to ensure they do not over-bake. The cookies should be golden at the edges.

7. Allow cookies to cool on the baking sheet for a few minutes before transferring to wire racks to cool completely, or enjoy warm.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- The modified recipe uses a gluten-free all-purpose flour blend and gluten-free certified chocolate chips and bacon, which may fulfill the gluten-free requirement. However, it is important to ensure that all components and manufacturing processes for these gluten-free ingredients are certified and cross-contamination-free. Cross-contamination is a risk if the gluten-free certification is not explicitly mentioned for all ingredients.
  
- If xanthan gum or any binder is used to compensate for the lack of gluten, it should ensure the texture is maintained. The recipe mentions adding xanthan gum but doesn’t specify a gluten-free certification for it when suggesting substitution in the blend. Confirming that the binder (if present) is also gluten-free is recommended.

Case 25-Title: Extra Flaky Pie Crust
Ingredients: ["3 c. flour", "1 tsp. salt", "1 Tbsp. vinegar", "1 1/4 c. lard", "1 egg, well beaten", "5 Tbsp. water"]
Directions: ["Blend flour, lard and salt; beat the egg and add the vinegar and the water to it and mix."]
Requirement: Wheat-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Gluten-Free Extra Flaky Pie Crust**

Ingredients:
- 2 1/2 c. gluten-free all-purpose flour blend (ensure it contains xanthan gum or add 1 tsp)
- 1 tsp. salt
- 1 Tbsp. white vinegar
- 1 1/4 c. cold unsalted butter, cubed
- 1 egg, well beaten
- 5 Tbsp. ice-cold water

Directions:
1. In a large bowl, combine the gluten-free all-purpose flour blend and salt.
2. Add the cubed cold butter to the flour mixture. Using a pastry cutter or your fingers, blend together until the mixture resembles coarse crumbs.
3. In a small bowl, beat the egg. Add the vinegar and ice-cold water to the egg and mix well.
4. Pour the egg mixture into the flour and butter mixture. Stir until the dough comes together. If needed, add a little more cold water, 1 tablespoon at a time, until the dough holds together.
5. Divide the dough into two equal parts, form each into a disk, wrap in plastic wrap, and refrigerate for at least 1 hour before rolling out.
6. Roll out the dough on a floured surface (use your gluten-free flour) to fit your pie pan, then proceed with your pie recipe as directed.
```

Case 26-Title: Bacon Quiche Biscuit Cups
Ingredients: ["1 (8 oz.) cream cheese, softened", "2 Tbsp. milk", "2 eggs", "1/2 c. shredded Swiss cheese", "2 Tbsp. chopped green onion", "1 (10 oz.) can refrigerator flaky biscuits", "5 slices bacon, crisply cooked and finely crumbled"]
Directions: ["In small bowl, beat cream cheese, milk and eggs on low speed until smooth.", "Stir in Swiss cheese and onions; set aside."]
Requirement: Sulfite-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Bacon Quiche Biscuit Cups (Sulfite-Free)**

Ingredients:
- 1 (8 oz.) sulfite-free cream cheese, softened
- 2 Tbsp. milk or a plant-based milk alternative (unsweetened almond or oat milk)
- 2 large eggs
- 1/2 c. shredded sulfite-free Swiss cheese
- 2 Tbsp. chopped green onion
- 1 batch sulfite-free homemade biscuit dough (see below for recipe)
- 5 slices sulfite-free bacon, crisply cooked and finely crumbled

**Homemade Sulfite-Free Biscuit Dough:**
- 2 c. all-purpose flour
- 1 Tbsp. baking powder
- 1/2 tsp. salt
- 1/4 c. cold unsalted butter, diced
- 3/4 c. milk or a plant-based milk alternative (unsweetened almond or oat milk)

Instructions:

1. **Prepare the Biscuit Dough:**
   - In a large bowl, whisk together the flour, baking powder, and salt.
   - Cut in the diced butter using a pastry blender or your fingers until the mixture resembles coarse crumbs.
   - Gradually add milk, stirring until a soft dough forms.
   - Turn the dough out onto a floured surface and knead gently, about 5-6 times, then roll out and cut into 12 small rounds.

2. **Prepare the Quiche Filling:**
   - In a small bowl, beat together the sulfite-free cream cheese, milk (or milk alternative), and eggs on low speed until smooth.
   - Stir in the shredded sulfite-free Swiss cheese and chopped green onion. Set aside.

3. **Assemble and Bake:**
   - Preheat the oven to 375°F (190°C).
   - Grease a muffin tin with a sulfite-free nonstick spray or line with muffin liners.
   - Press a round of biscuit dough into each muffin cup, ensuring it covers the bottom and up the sides.
   - Fill each cup with the cream cheese mixture, then top with crumbled sulfite-free bacon.
   - Bake for 20-25 minutes, or until the eggs are set and the biscuits are golden brown.
   - Allow to cool in the pan for 5 minutes before removing to a wire rack to cool slightly before serving.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

**Edibility and Nutritional Sense:**
The modified recipe makes nutritional and edible sense with appropriate substitutions for a sulfite-free version.

**Ingredient Safety:**
The recipe specifies the use of "sulfite-free" versions of certain ingredients, like cream cheese, Swiss cheese, and bacon. However, the use of milk alternatives (almond or oat milk) introduces potential risks of cross-contamination for those with nut allergies (almond milk) or gluten sensitivities (oat milk unless certified gluten-free). Ensure that all milk alternatives and other ingredients are certified sulfite-free and free from cross-contamination.

**Requirement Fulfillment:**
The requirement for a sulfite-free recipe seems to be fulfilled as the recipe specifies the use of sulfite-free alternatives. However, it's essential to verify that all processed ingredients like cream cheese, Swiss cheese, and bacon are indeed sulfite-free, as natural variations or cross-contamination can be a risk.

**Cooking Steps:**
The cooking steps are logical and feasible with the modified ingredients and allow for the preparation of the dish as described.

Case 27-Title: Pasta with Anchovies and Tomatoes
Ingredients: ["1 pound bowtie-shaped pasta (farfalle)", "3/4 cup finely chopped onion", "1 garlic clove, minced", "2 tablespoons olive oil", "a 2-ounce can flat anchovy fillets, drained and minced", "a 28- to 32-ounce can tomatoes, drained, reserving juice, and chopped", "1 tablespoon balsamic vinegar", "1/2 teaspoon dried hot red pepper flakes", "2 tablespoons drained capers, chopped", "2 ounces thinly sliced prosciutto, chopped (about 1/2 cup)", "1/4 cup finely chopped fresh basil or parsley leaves (wash and dry before chopping), or to taste", "Accompaniment: freshly grated Parmesan"]
Directions: ["In a 6-quart kettle bring 5 quarts salted water to a boil for pasta.", "In a large skillet cook onion and garlic in oil over moderately low heat, stirring, until onion is softened.", "Add anchovies and cook, stirring, 1 minute.", "Add tomatoes with reserved juice, vinegar, and red pepper flakes and cook, stirring occasionally, until slightly thickened.", "Add capers, prosciutto, basil or parsley, and salt and pepper to taste and keep warm.", "Cook pasta in boiling water until al dente and drain in a colander.", "In a large bowl toss pasta with sauce and serve with Parmesan."]
Requirement: Gluten-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
### Modified Recipe: Gluten-Free Pasta with Anchovies and Tomatoes

**Ingredients:**
- 1 pound gluten-free bowtie-shaped pasta (farfalle) or similar shape, such as gluten-free fusilli
- 3/4 cup finely chopped onion
- 1 garlic clove, minced
- 2 tablespoons olive oil
- 2-ounce can flat anchovy fillets, drained and minced
- 28- to 32-ounce can tomatoes, drained, reserving juice, and chopped
- 1 tablespoon balsamic vinegar
- 1/2 teaspoon dried hot red pepper flakes
- 2 tablespoons drained capers, chopped
- 2 ounces thinly sliced prosciutto, chopped (about 1/2 cup)
- 1/4 cup finely chopped fresh basil or parsley leaves (wash and dry before chopping), or to taste
- Accompaniment: freshly grated Parmesan (ensure gluten-free)

**Instructions:**
1. In a 6-quart kettle bring 5 quarts salted water to a boil for pasta.
2. In a large skillet, cook onion and garlic in olive oil over moderately low heat, stirring, until the onion is softened.
3. Add anchovies and cook, stirring for 1 minute.
4. Add tomatoes with reserved juice, balsamic vinegar, and red pepper flakes and cook, stirring occasionally, until slightly thickened.
5. Add capers, prosciutto, basil or parsley, and salt and pepper to taste, and keep warm.
6. Cook gluten-free pasta in boiling water until al dente and drain in a colander.
7. In a large bowl, toss pasta with sauce and serve with freshly grated Parmesan.
```

```markdown
**Dish Name:** Mustard Plus Glazed Pork Chops (Dairy-Free)

**Modified Recipe:**
Ingredients:
- 3 tablespoons orange marmalade
- 2 tablespoons tamari (gluten-free soy sauce), or coconut aminos for a soy-free option
- 1 teaspoon Dijon mustard (ensure dairy-free, coarse grained preferred)
- 1/4 teaspoon crushed red pepper flakes (optional)
- 1/4 cup water
- 4 center cut pork loin chops with bone (1/2 inch thick), trimmed
- Black pepper, to taste
- 1 teaspoon grapeseed oil or avocado oil (ensure monocular source)
- 1/2 cup thin sliced green onion

7. Cover the pan and let it simmer until the chops are cooked through, about 15 minutes.
8. Stir in the green onions just before serving.
9. Arrange the pork chops on a platter and garnish with slices of orange.
```

```markdown
### Modified Simple Ranch Beans

**Ingredients:**
- 2 (15 ounce) cans ranch style beans
- 1 (15 ounce) can baked beans
- 1 large green bell pepper, chopped
- 1 large onion, chopped
- 1/2 lb turkey bacon, cooked and crumbled
- Optional: 1 chopped jalapeño pepper for spicier beans

**Directions:**
1. In a skillet, sauté the chopped green bell pepper and onion over medium heat for 8 to 10 minutes until softened.
2. Transfer the sautéed vegetables to a crock pot.
3. Add the ranch style beans, baked beans, and turkey bacon to the crock pot.
4. Cook on low heat for 4 to 6 hours until the flavors meld together.
5. Season with salt and pepper to taste.
6. For added heat, stir in the chopped jalapeño pepper if desired.
```

Case 31-Title: Spinach and Rice Casserole
Ingredients: ["12 cup rice, uncooked", "1 cup butter", "13 cup flour", "1 quart half-and-half or 1 quart milk", "3 eggs", "2 lbs spinach, cooked,drained and chopped", "14 cup green onion, chopped", "1 12 cups feta cheese, crumbled", "14 cup parmesan cheese", "1 tablespoon paprika", "salt and pepper"]
Directions: ["Set oven to 350 degrees.", "Grease a 13\" x 9\" baking pan.", "Cook 1-1/2 cups rice according to directions; set aside.", "In a heavy-bottomed saucepan, melt 1 cup butter; add in flour, stir until thoroughly mixed (about 2 minutes), allow to cool slightly.", "In the microwave, heat the half and half until just to boiling or to a\"simmer\" (I do this in the microwave so that the milk doesn't scald bottom of pot, but you could simmer it in the pot, just watch not to burn bottom of pot!", ").", "Pour in the simmering half and half into a saucepan.", "Add flour mixture into the milk mixture a little at a time, whisking to break up all the lumps.", "Then whisk in the eggs, until creamy and smooth (about 10-15 minutes).", "Place the cooked and drained spinach in bottom of casserole dish.", "Add rice, Feta cheese and green onions spreading evenly over spinach.", "Sprinkle with salt and pepper to taste.", "Pour the cream sauce over the top.", "Sprinkle with Parmesan cheese and paprika.", "Bake for 20-25 minutes."]
Requirement: Mustard-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Spinach and Rice Casserole (Mustard-Free)**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 1/2 cups rice, uncooked
- 1 cup unsalted butter
- 1/3 cup all-purpose flour
- 1 quart oat milk or any other non-dairy milk that is mustard-free
- 3 eggs
- 2 lbs spinach, cooked, drained, and chopped
- 1/4 cup green onion, chopped
- 1 1/2 cups feta cheese, crumbled
- 1/4 cup parmesan cheese
- 1 tablespoon sweet paprika
- Salt and pepper to taste

**Instructions:**
1. Preheat the oven to 350 degrees F (175 degrees C).
2. Grease a 13"x9" baking pan.
3. Cook 1 1/2 cups rice according to package directions; set aside.
4. In a heavy-bottomed saucepan, melt the unsalted butter; add in the flour and stir until thoroughly mixed (about 2 minutes). Allow to cool slightly.
5. Heat the oat milk just to boiling or to a simmer (this can be done in the microwave to prevent scalding).
6. Pour the simmering oat milk into the saucepan.
7. Add the flour mixture into the oat milk, a little at a time, whisking to break up all the lumps.
8. Then whisk in the eggs until creamy and smooth (about 10-15 minutes).
9. Place the cooked and drained spinach at the bottom of the casserole dish.
10. Add rice, feta cheese, and green onions, spreading evenly over the spinach.
11. Sprinkle with salt and pepper to taste.
12. Pour the cream sauce over the top.
13. Sprinkle with parmesan cheese and sweet paprika.
14. Bake for 20-25 minutes.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

The modified recipe claims to be mustard-free. However, there's a potential ambiguity regarding the feta cheese and Parmesan cheese. Some brands may include additives or preservatives that could potentially contain mustard or cross-contaminate with mustard during processing, depending on manufacturing practices. 

To fully satisfy the mustard-free requirement, it is important to ensure that all ingredients, particularly processed ones like cheese, are explicitly labeled or certified as mustard-free to avoid cross-contamination risks.

```markdown
**Modified Cornish Game Hen Recipe (With Wild Rice)**

**Ingredients:**
- 2 Cornish game hens
- 1 box wild rice blend (ensure it's sesame-free; wild and white mixed or wild and brown mixed)
- 1/2 cup raisins (optional)
- Salt for flavoring
- 2 tablespoons olive oil or melted unsalted butter (ensure it's sesame-free)

**Directions:**
1. Preheat the oven to 350°F (175°C).
2. Wash the Cornish game hens thoroughly.
3. Sprinkle each hen with salt, being sure to season the inside of the cavity as well as the entire outside of the bird.
4. Prepare the rice according to the directions on the box. Ensure the rice blend is free from any sesame or sesame-derived flavorings.
5. When the rice is done, add the raisins and mix together.
6. Stuff each hen with the rice mixture.
7. Place the hens in a roasting pan. You may wrap them in foil first if desired.
8. Bake the hens in the preheated oven for 45 minutes.
9. Remove the hens and baste each bird with 2 tablespoons of melted unsalted butter or olive oil, ensuring the product is sesame-free.
10. Return the hens to the oven and continue baking until they are golden brown and tender, usually about 15 to 20 minutes longer.
11. Ensure the internal temperature reaches at least 165°F (75°C) before serving.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- Olive oil and unsalted butter must be carefully sourced to confirm they are free from sesame contamination. Look for labels or certifications that indicate they are produced in a sesame-free environment.
- Be vigilant about checking that the roasting pan, foil, and any utensils used have not come into contact with sesame-containing products to prevent cross-contact.

The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Catatini Recipe**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 cup sliced nitrate-free turkey pepperoni
- 1 lb. ground turkey
- 1 jar sulfite-free spaghetti sauce
- 1 cup shredded dairy-free cheese (e.g., a blend made from coconut oil and potato starch)
- 1 pkg. gluten-free elbow noodles
- Salt and pepper to taste

**Instructions:**
1. Boil the gluten-free elbow noodles until tender; drain.
```

```markdown
**Modified Black Chocolate Cake Recipe**

**Ingredients:**

- 2 c. All-purpose flour
- 2 c. Granulated sugar
- 1 c. Unsweetened cocoa powder
- 1 pinch Salt
- 8 Tbsp. Canola oil (up to 10)
- 2 tsp Baking soda
- 2 c. Boiling water
- 1 x Egg
- 1 tsp Vanilla extract (up to 2)
  
**For Larger Cake:**

- 3 c. All-purpose flour
- 3 c. Granulated sugar
- 1 1/2 c. Unsweetened cocoa powder
- 1 pinch Salt
- 14 Tbsp. Canola oil (up to 15)
- 3 tsp Baking soda
- 3 c. Boiling water
- 2 x Large eggs
- 2 1/2 tsp Vanilla extract

**For Frosting:**

- 3 Tbsp. All-purpose flour
- 1/2 c. Whole milk
- 1/2 c. Butter (soy-free)
- 1/2 c. Granulated sugar
- 1/2 tsp Vanilla extract (up to 1)
- 1 pinch Salt

**Instructions:**

1. Preheat your oven to 350°F (175°C). Grease and flour a baking pan.
2. In a large bowl, mix flour, sugar, and cocoa powder together.
3. Add a healthy pinch of salt and stir again.
4. Add canola oil and stir well.
5. In a separate bowl, stir baking soda into the boiling water, then quickly add this mixture to the large bowl. Stir well.
6. Add in the egg(s) and vanilla extract; stir until well combined.
7. Pour batter into the prepared baking pan. Bake for about 1 hour, or until a toothpick inserted comes out clean.

**For Frosting:**

1. In a saucepan, place flour and gradually whisk in whole milk until smooth.
2. Heat over low flame, stirring constantly, until the mixture forms a thick paste. Cool well.
3. In a separate bowl, beat butter and sugar with an electric mixer until well blended.
4. Add the cooled flour/milk paste to the butter and sugar mixture.
5. Beat with a mixer until light and fluffy, about 5 minutes.
6. Add a healthy pinch of salt and vanilla extract; beat again briefly.
7. Frost the cake once it is completely cooled.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

These products could be at risk of cross-contamination if not specifically labeled soy-free. Ingredients: ["1 package (1/4 ounce) active dry yeast", "1/2 cup warm water (110\u00b0 to 115\u00b0)", "8-1/2 teaspoons honey, divided", "2 cups whole wheat flour", "3/4 cup warm milk (110\u00b0 to 115\u00b0)", "6 tablespoons butter, softened, divided", "1 egg", "1 teaspoon salt", "1-3/4 to 2-1/4 cups all-purpose flour", "1/4 cup grated Parmesan cheese", "1/4 teaspoon garlic salt"]
Directions: ["In a large bowl, dissolve yeast in warm water. Stir in 2 teaspoons honey; let stand for 5 minutes. Add the whole wheat flour, milk, 2 tablespoons butter, egg, salt, remaining honey and 1 cup all-purpose flour. Beat on medium speed for 3 minutes. Stir in enough remaining all-purpose flour to form a soft dough.", "Turn onto a floured surface; knead until smooth and elastic, about 6-8 minutes. Place in a greased bowl, turning once to grease top. Cover and let rise in a warm place until doubled, about 1 hour.", "Punch dough down. Knead on a floured surface for 30 seconds. Requirement: Gluten-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Dish Name:** Gluten-Free Savory Crescents

**Ingredients:**
- 1 package (1/4 ounce) active dry yeast
- 1/2 cup warm water (110° to 115°)
- 8-1/2 teaspoons honey, divided
- 2 cups gluten-free whole grain flour blend (ensure it includes xanthan gum or guar gum)
- 3/4 cup warm almond milk (110° to 115°)
- 6 tablespoons gluten-free margarine, softened, divided
- 1 egg
- 1 teaspoon salt
- 1-3/4 to 2-1/4 cups gluten-free all-purpose flour blend (ensure it includes xanthan gum or guar gum)
- 1/4 cup grated lactose-free Parmesan cheese
- 1/4 teaspoon garlic salt

**Directions:**
1. In a large bowl, dissolve yeast in warm water. Stir in 2 teaspoons honey; let stand for 5 minutes. Add the gluten-free whole grain flour, almond milk, 2 tablespoons margarine, egg, salt, remaining honey, and 1 cup gluten-free all-purpose flour. Beat on medium speed for 3 minutes. Stir in enough remaining gluten-free all-purpose flour to form a soft dough.
2. Turn onto a floured surface using the gluten-free flour blend; knead until smooth and elastic, about 6-8 minutes. Place in a greased bowl, turning once to grease top. Cover and let rise in a warm place until doubled, about 1 hour.
3. Punch dough down. Knead on a floured surface for 30 seconds. Roll into a 12-in. circle. Melt remaining margarine; brush over dough. Combine lactose-free Parmesan cheese and garlic salt; sprinkle over dough.
4. Cut into 16 wedges. Roll up wedges from the wide end and place with pointed end down on a greased baking sheet. Curve ends to form a crescent shape. Cover and let rise in a warm place until doubled, about 20 minutes.
5. Bake at 400° for 12-15 minutes or until golden brown. Remove from pans to wire racks to cool.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- The requirement for gluten-free is mostly addressed with gluten-free whole grain flour blend and gluten-free all-purpose flour blend. However, it is crucial to ensure these blends are explicitly certified gluten-free to avoid potential contamination. Make sure the flour blends are from a trusted supplier and explicitly state their gluten-free certification as cross-contamination risks in gluten-free products are a concern.

- Almond milk should be verified as gluten-free, as some brands might not be certified or could have cross-contamination risks. Ensure that the almond milk used is labeled and certified gluten-free.

Ingredients: ["1 medium butternut squash, peeled, seeded and cut into large dice", "2 medium red apples (look for sweet/tart and crisp), peeled, cored and cut into large dice", "1 teaspoon lemon juice", "1 small onion, diced", "1 medium clove garlic, minced", "11/2 teaspoons coarse salt", "11/2 teaspoons ground cumin", "1/2 teaspoon ground coriander", "1/2 teaspoon smoky Spanish paprika", "2 cups chicken or vegetable stock", "11/2 cups water", "Salt and pepper, to taste", "1 sprig cilantro, optional for garnish", "4 tablespoons light sour cream, optional for garnish"]
Directions: ["Preheat oven to 425\u00b0F.", "Toss diced squash with 1 Tbsp of olive oil and spread out on foil-lined baking sheet. Lightly sprinkle pinch of coarse salt over squash. Cook for 30-40 minutes, until squash is fork tender and lightly caramelized.", "While squash is cooking, toss diced apple with lemon juice, and set aside.", "Heat olive oil over medium-low heat and add onion. Season with additional salt and pepper, to taste. Requirement: Egg-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Smoky Butternut Squash and Apple Soup**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 medium butternut squash, peeled, seeded and cut into large dice
- 2 medium red apples (sweet/tart and crisp), peeled, cored and cut into large dice
- 1 teaspoon lemon juice
- 1 small onion, diced
- 1 medium clove garlic, minced
- 1½ teaspoons coarse salt
- 1½ teaspoons ground cumin
- ½ teaspoon ground coriander
- ½ teaspoon smoky Spanish paprika
- 2 cups vegetable stock (ensure it's egg-free)
- 1½ cups water
- Salt and pepper, to taste
- 1 sprig cilantro, optional for garnish
- 4 tablespoons coconut yogurt or dairy-free yogurt alternative, optional for garnish

**Instructions:**
1. Preheat oven to 425°F.
2. Toss diced squash with 1 tablespoon of olive oil and spread out on a foil-lined baking sheet. Lightly sprinkle a pinch of coarse salt over squash. Cook for 30-40 minutes, until squash is fork tender and lightly caramelized.
3. While squash is cooking, toss diced apple with lemon juice, and set aside.
4. Heat a tablespoon of olive oil over medium-low heat and add onion. Sauté for 3-4 minutes, until translucent. Add garlic, salt, and spices and sauté for 2-3 more minutes, being careful not to burn garlic.
5. Add apples, water, and vegetable stock, bring to a boil, then reduce heat and simmer until apples are fork tender, about 10 minutes.
6. Purée roasted squash in batches with the apple mixture, in a food processor or blender, until smooth, and return to saucepan. Season with additional salt and pepper, to taste. Heat over low, thinning with more water if necessary to get desired consistency, for 5-7 minutes before serving.
7. To serve, ladle into shallow bowls, and top each serving with 1 tablespoon of coconut yogurt or dairy-free yogurt alternative (optional) and a sprig of cilantro (optional). For extra color and flavor, sprinkle additional smoky paprika over the soup.
```

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Grilled Shrimp (Sulfite-Free)**

**Ingredients:**
- 4 cloves Garlic, Roasted
- 1 Tablespoon Olive Oil
- 2 teaspoons Dried Mint Leaves, Divided
- 17 whole Raw Shrimp
- 2 teaspoons Coconut Aminos (ensure sulfite-free)
- 6 teaspoons Cold Water
- 1 teaspoon Homemade Hoisin Sauce (see note)
- 1/4 teaspoons Homemade Chili Garlic Paste (see note)
- 2 teaspoons Pure Maple Syrup
- 1 teaspoon Fresh Lime Juice

**Homemade Hoisin Sauce:**
- 1 tablespoon Peanut Butter or Sunflower Seed Butter
- 2 teaspoons Coconut Aminos (ensure sulfite-free)
- 1 teaspoon Rice Vinegar (ensure sulfite-free)
- 1 teaspoon Molasses
- Pinch of Garlic Powder
- Pinch of Ground Black Pepper

**Homemade Chili Garlic Paste:**
- 1 Fresh Red Chili, minced (remove seeds for less heat)
- 1 clove Garlic, minced
- 1 teaspoon Apple Cider Vinegar (ensure sulfite-free)
- Pinch of Salt

**Directions:**
1. To make the homemade hoisin sauce, mix peanut butter, coconut aminos, rice vinegar, molasses, garlic powder, and ground black pepper in a small bowl until smooth. Set aside.
2. To make the homemade chili garlic paste, combine minced chili, garlic, apple cider vinegar, and salt in a small bowl. Mix until well combined. Set aside.
3. Crush the roasted garlic cloves with a fork. In a large bowl, mix the garlic with olive oil and 1 teaspoon of dried mint.
4. Add the raw shrimp to the bowl and toss to coat. Cover and refrigerate to marinate overnight.
5. In a separate bowl with a cover, mix coconut aminos, water, homemade hoisin sauce, homemade chili garlic paste, maple syrup, and lime juice. Refrigerate until the next day.
6. When ready to cook, preheat the grill or a pan over medium-high heat.
7. Grill or pan-fry the shrimp for 2-3 minutes on each side or until they are fully cooked.
8. Serve the shrimp with the prepared sauce. Enjoy!
```

**Note:** Be sure all ingredients, such as coconut aminos, rice vinegar, and apple cider vinegar, are explicitly labeled as sulfite-free to meet dietary restrictions.

```markdown
### Modified Jalapeno Salsa Dona

#### Ingredients:
- 12 large jalapenos
- 6 cloves roasted garlic
- 1/4 cup extra-virgin olive oil
- 1 tablespoon apple cider vinegar
- Salt to taste

#### Directions:
1. Rinse the jalapenos and arrange them on a baking sheet.
2. Turn the oven to broil.
3. Roast the peppers under the broiler until lightly browned, turning so all sides are browned.
4. Turn off the heat and let the peppers sit for about 10 minutes.

6. Place the peppers, garlic, olive oil, and apple cider vinegar in a blender or food processor.
```

```markdown
**Praline Brownies - Modified Recipe (Fish-Free)**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 (20 ounce) box regular fudge brownie mix (13x9 pan size) - ensure it's fish-free and does not contain fish allergens
- 1/4 cup water
- 1/2 cup softened unsalted butter
- 3 eggs
- 1/2 cup firmly packed brown sugar
- 1/2 cup chopped pecans
- 2 tablespoons unsalted butter, melted

**Instructions:**
1. Preheat the oven to 350°F (175°C).
2. In a mixing bowl, prepare the brownies according to the package directions, using 1/4 cup of water, 1/2 cup of softened unsalted butter, and 3 eggs.
3. Spread the brownie mixture into a greased 13x9 inch baking pan.
4. In a separate bowl, combine the brown sugar, chopped pecans, and 2 tablespoons of melted unsalted butter.
5. Sprinkle the brown sugar and pecan mixture evenly over the brownie batter.
6. Bake in the preheated oven for 25-30 minutes, or until a toothpick inserted 2 inches from the side comes out clean.
7. Allow to cool completely in the pan before cutting into bars.
```

Case 50-Title: Triple-Citrus Cupcakes
Ingredients: ["3 1/3 cups all-purpose flour", "2 teaspoons coarse salt", "1 pound (4 sticks) unsalted butter, room temperature", "2 cups sugar", "3 tablespoons finely grated lemon zest (from 3 lemons)", "3 tablespoons finely grated orange zest (from 2 oranges)", "3 tablespoons finely grated lime zest, plus more for garnish (from about 3 limes)", "1 teaspoon pure vanilla extract", "9 large eggs, room temperature", "Citrus Glaze (made with lime juice and zest; page 315)"]
Directions: ["Preheat oven to 325F.", "Line standard muffin tins with paper liners.", "Whisk together flour and salt.", "With an electric mixer on medium-high speed, cream butter and sugar until pale and fluffy, scraping down sides of bowl every few minutes.", "Add citrus zests.", "Reduce speed to medium, and add vanilla.", "Add eggs, three at a time, beating until incorporated, scraping down sides of bowl as needed.", "Reduce speed to low.", "Add flour mixture in four batches, beating until completely incorporated after each.", "Divide batter evenly among lined cups, filling each three-quarters full; tap pans on countertop once to distribute batter.", "Bake, rotating tins halfway through, until a cake tester inserted in centers comes out clean, about 20 minutes.", "Transfer tins to wire racks to cool 10 minutes; turn out cupcakes onto racks and let cool completely.", "Cupcakes can be stored up to 2 days at room temperature, or frozen up to 2 months, in airtight containers.", "To finish, dip tops of cupcakes in glaze, then turn over quickly and garnish with zest.", "Cupcakes are best eaten the day they are glazed; keep at room temperature until ready to serve."]
Requirement: Dairy-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Dish Name:** Dairy-Free Triple-Citrus Cupcakes

**Ingredients:**
- 3 1/3 cups all-purpose flour
- 2 teaspoons coarse salt
- 1 pound (2 cups) dairy-free butter substitute, room temperature (e.g., coconut oil or vegan margarine)
- 2 cups sugar
- 3 tablespoons finely grated lemon zest (from 3 lemons)
- 3 tablespoons finely grated orange zest (from 2 oranges)
- 3 tablespoons finely grated lime zest, plus more for garnish (from about 3 limes)
- 1 teaspoon pure vanilla extract
- 9 large eggs, room temperature
- Citrus Glaze (made with lime juice and zest; page 315)

**Instructions:**
1. Preheat oven to 325°F.
2. Line standard muffin tins with paper liners.
3. Whisk together flour and salt.
4. With an electric mixer on medium-high speed, cream the dairy-free butter substitute and sugar until pale and fluffy, scraping down sides of bowl every few minutes.
5. Add citrus zests.
6. Reduce speed to medium, and add vanilla.
7. Add eggs, three at a time, beating until incorporated, scraping down sides of bowl as needed.
8. Reduce speed to low.
9. Add flour mixture in four batches, beating until completely incorporated after each batch.
10. Divide batter evenly among lined cups, filling each three-quarters full; tap pans on countertop once to release air bubbles.
11. Bake, rotating tins halfway through, until a cake tester inserted in centers comes out clean, about 20 minutes.
12. Transfer tins to wire racks to cool for 10 minutes; turn out cupcakes onto racks and let cool completely.
13. To finish, dip tops of cupcakes in glaze, then turn over quickly and garnish with additional lime zest.
14. Cupcakes are best eaten the day they are glazed; keep at room temperature until ready to serve.
```

Case 51-Title: Blackberry And Mint Chocolate Muffins
Ingredients: ["2/3 cups Cocoa Powder", "1-3/4 cup Flour", "1-1/4 cup Brown Sugar", "1 teaspoon Baking Powder", "1 teaspoon Baking Soda", "3/4 teaspoons Salt", "2 whole Large Eggs", "1 cup Milk", "2 teaspoons Vanilla", "2 teaspoons Vinegar", "1 cup Butter, Melted", "1 cup Fresh Blackberries, Halved", "1 Tablespoon Fresh Spearmint, Chopped"]
Directions: ["Preheat oven to 400\u00b0F.", "Whisk together all of the dry ingredients (cocoa powder through salt) in a medium-sized mixing bowl. In a separate, smaller bowl, combine eggs, milk, vanilla and vinegar. Add wet ingredients into dry, adding the melted butter as well. Whisk just to combine, not worrying about any small lumps that may exist in the batter. Fold in blackberries and chopped mint.", "Spoon the batter into two 12-count baking cup lined muffin tins and bake in at 400\u00b0F for 20 minutes.", "(Recipe adapted from Dorie Greenspan.)"]
Requirement: Shellfish-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Blackberry And Mint Chocolate Muffins**

**Ingredients:**
- 2/3 cup Cocoa Powder
- 1-3/4 cup Flour
- 1-1/4 cup Brown Sugar
- 1 teaspoon Baking Powder
- 1 teaspoon Baking Soda
- 3/4 teaspoons Salt
- 2 whole Large Eggs
- 1 cup Milk (or plant-based milk for dairy-free)
- 2 teaspoons Vanilla Extract
- 2 teaspoons Apple Cider Vinegar
- 1 cup Unsalted Butter, Melted (or dairy-free margarine for dairy-free)
- 1 cup Fresh Blackberries, Halved
- 1 Tablespoon Fresh Spearmint, Chopped

**Directions:**
1. Preheat oven to 400°F.
2. Whisk together all of the dry ingredients (cocoa powder through salt) in a medium-sized mixing bowl.
3. In a separate, smaller bowl, combine eggs, milk, vanilla extract, and apple cider vinegar.
4. Add wet ingredients into dry ingredients, along with the melted butter. Whisk just to combine, not worrying about any small lumps that may exist in the batter.
5. Fold in the blackberries and chopped spearmint.
6. Spoon the batter into two 12-count baking cup-lined muffin tins.
7. Bake at 400°F for 20 minutes or until a toothpick inserted into the center of a muffin comes out clean.

```
