Case 173-Title: Chicken El Paso(Makes 4 Servings)  
Ingredients: ["4 boneless chicken breasts", "1 1/2 c. long grain rice", "3 c. cold water", "1 to 2 c. salsa (barbecue sauce can be substituted)", "2 c. shredded Colby cheese"]
Directions: ["Preheat oven to broil.", "Tenderize the chicken with a tenderizing mallet and season to taste.", "Put the chicken on a broiling pan and broil for 10 minutes on each side.", "While the chicken is broiling, put the rice and water into a medium size saucepan.", "Bring the rice and water to a boil, cover and reduce heat to a simmer for 15 minutes.", "Once the rice and chicken are cooked, place a bed of rice on each serving plate.", "Place a broiled chicken breast on each bed of rice and pour a generous amount of salsa (or barbecue sauce) over the chicken and rice.", "Finally, top each serving with 1/4 of the shredded cheese and place into the microwave oven for 1 minute (or until the cheese melts).", "Serve while hot and enjoy!"]
Requirement: Sesame-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Chicken El Paso (Sesame-Free)**

**Ingredients:**
- 4 boneless chicken breasts
- 1 1/2 cups long grain rice
- 3 cups cold water
- 1 to 2 cups sesame-free salsa (ensure label specifies no sesame ingredients)
- 2 cups shredded Colby cheese
- Salt and black pepper to taste

**Directions:**
1. Preheat the oven to broil.
2. Tenderize the chicken with a tenderizing mallet and season with salt and black pepper.
3. Place the chicken on a broiling pan and broil for 10 minutes on each side until fully cooked.
4. While the chicken is broiling, combine the rice and water in a medium saucepan.
5. Bring the rice and water to a boil, cover, and reduce heat to a simmer for 15 minutes or until the rice is tender and water is absorbed.
6. Once the rice and chicken are cooked, place a bed of rice on each serving plate.
7. Place a broiled chicken breast on each bed of rice and pour a generous amount of sesame-free salsa over the chicken and rice.
8. Top each serving with 1/4 of the shredded Colby cheese.
9. Place the prepared dishes into the microwave oven for 1 minute, or until the cheese melts.
10. Serve while hot and enjoy!
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

- Verify that all tools and utensils used in the preparation process are free from any sesame contamination.

Ingredients: ["2 pkg. frozen broccoli (chopped)", "1/2 c. chopped onion", "6 Tbsp. margarine", "2 Tbsp. flour", "1/2 c. water", "salt to taste", "1 (8 oz.) jar Cheez Whiz", "3 eggs, well beaten", "1 stack Ritz crackers, crushed into crumbs"]

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Cheese Broccoli Recipe**

Ingredients:
- 2 packages frozen broccoli (chopped)
- 1/2 cup chopped onion
- 6 tablespoons vegan butter
- 2 tablespoons all-purpose flour
- 1/2 cup water
- Salt to taste
- 1 cup nutritional yeast (for cheese flavor)
- 3 eggs, well beaten
- 1 stack Ritz-style gluten-free crackers, crushed into crumbs

Directions:
1. Thaw broccoli and drain well.
2. In a saucepan, sauté onion in 4 tablespoons of vegan butter until translucent.
3. Stir in flour to form a paste.
4. Gradually add water, stirring continuously over low heat until the mixture thickens.
5. Add salt to taste.

7. In a large bowl, combine the sauce with broccoli and beaten eggs, mixing gently until well blended.
8. Transfer the mixture into a greased casserole dish.
9. Top with crushed gluten-free crackers.
10. Dot with remaining 2 tablespoons of vegan butter.
11. Bake at 350°F for 30 minutes.
```

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Celery-Free Royal Icing**

**Ingredients:**
- 3 ounces aquafaba (ensure it is labeled as certified celery-free, sourced from a dedicated facility)
- 1 teaspoon pure vanilla extract
- 4 cups confectioners' sugar

**Instructions:**
1. In the large bowl of a stand mixer, combine the aquafaba and vanilla extract. Beat on medium speed until the mixture becomes frothy.

3. Increase the mixer speed to high. Beat the mixture until it forms stiff, glossy peaks. This process should take approximately 5 to 7 minutes.
4. If desired, add food coloring to achieve the preferred hue.
5. For immediate use, transfer the icing to a pastry bag or a heavy-duty storage bag to pipe as desired. If using a storage bag, clip the corner to use as a makeshift piping bag.
6. Store any unused icing in an airtight container in the refrigerator for up to 3 days.
```

Case 178-Title: Amazing Salmon Blender Souffle
Ingredients: ["Butter or margarine", "Bread crumbs", "8 ounces smoked salmon or 1 (7 1/2-ounce) can red salmon", "6 eggs", "12 ounces cottage cheese", "2 tablespoons lemon juice", "1 teaspoons Dijon mustard", "1/2 -cup chopped red onion", "1/4 -cup fresh dill"]
Directions: ["Preheat oven to 350 degrees.", "Butter and dust with bread crumbs a 1-quart souffle dish or 4 (8-ounce) ramekins.", "Coarsely chop smoked salmon and put aside, or if using canned salmon, thoroughly drain the salmon.", "In a bowl, clean bones and skin from salmon.", "Break it into fine pieces with a fork.", "Set aside.", "Place all remaining ingredients in a blender container.", "Cover and blend at medium speed for about 30 seconds.", "Blend at high speed for another 10 to15 seconds.", "Stir the egg mixture into the bowl with the salmon.", "Pour the mixture into the prepared souffle dish or spoon the mixture into the prepared ramekins including an equal amount of salmon pieces in each.", "Bake for 45 minutes to 50 minutes on a cookie sheet, until puffy and delicately browned.", "Don't open oven door for at least 30 minutes.", "Serve immediately."]
Requirement: Dairy-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Dish Name:** Dairy-Free Amazing Salmon Blender Souffle

**Ingredients:**
- Substitute for butter or margarine: 2 tablespoons olive oil
- 2 tablespoons dairy-free bread crumbs
- 8 ounces smoked salmon or 1 (7 1/2-ounce) can red salmon
- 6 eggs
- Substitute for cottage cheese: 12 ounces silken tofu, drained
- 2 tablespoons lemon juice
- 1 teaspoon Dijon mustard
- 1/2 cup chopped red onion
- 1/4 cup fresh dill

**Directions:**
1. Preheat oven to 350 degrees F.
2. Use olive oil to grease a 1-quart souffle dish or 4 (8-ounce) ramekins. Dust with dairy-free bread crumbs.
3. Coarsely chop smoked salmon and set aside, or if using canned salmon, thoroughly drain the salmon and clean bones and skin from it. Break it into fine pieces with a fork. Set aside.
4. Place silken tofu, eggs, lemon juice, Dijon mustard, chopped red onion, and fresh dill in a blender container.
5. Cover and blend at medium speed for about 30 seconds, then blend at high speed for another 10 to 15 seconds.
6. Stir the egg mixture into the bowl with the salmon, mixing well.
7. Pour the mixture into the prepared souffle dish or spoon the mixture into the prepared ramekins, ensuring an equal amount of salmon pieces in each.
8. Bake for 45 to 50 minutes on a cookie sheet, until puffy and delicately browned. Do not open the oven door for at least 30 minutes.
9. Serve immediately.
```

```markdown
**Modified Recipe for Corn-Free Sausage Cheese Grits Casserole**

Ingredients:
- 4 c. water
- 1/2 tsp. salt
- 1 c. millet (or quinoa), rinsed and drained
- 1 1/2 c. (6 oz.) grated sharp Cheddar cheese, divided
- 1/4 c. (1/2 stick) unsalted butter
- 4 eggs, lightly beaten
- 1/2 c. unsweetened almond milk (ensure it is free from corn derivatives)
- 1 lb. sausage, browned and drained (ensure corn-free, verify ingredients carefully)

Directions:
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (175°C).
2. Grease a 3-quart baking dish.
3. Bring water and salt to a boil in a large saucepan.
4. Slowly pour in millet (or quinoa).
5. Cover, reduce heat, and cook for 15-20 minutes (for quinoa, 12-15 minutes), stirring occasionally, until the grains are tender and water is absorbed.
6. Remove from heat. Stir in 1 cup of cheese and butter until melted.
7. Add eggs, almond milk, and sausage; blend well.
8. Pour mixture into the prepared dish.
9. Sprinkle with the remaining cheese.
10. Bake 1 hour or until cheese is golden brown. Cool for 10 minutes before serving.

Makes 6 to 8 servings.
```

The same rings true for the sausage; it should be explicitly labeled corn-free to ensure safety for someone with a corn allergy. Any ambiguous information about ingredient processing can lead to cross-contamination potential, warranting verification with manufacturers.

Proceed with caution and ensure all ingredients are rigorously checked to truly cater to the corn-free requirement.

Heat until fragrant, about 1 minute.", "Add shallot and celery and saute for 1 minute, stirring constantly.", "Add shrimp, reduce heat to low, and cook for 5 minutes, stirring constantly.", "Remove from heat and cool about 15 minutes.", "In a food processor or blender, process the egg for about 30 seconds. Using kitchen shears, cut off the front of the crab, about 1/2 inch behind the eyes and mouth. Squeeze out the contents of the sack located directly behind the cut just made.", "Season the crab with salt and pepper.", "I'm partial to a charcoal grill because it adds a smokiness I find pretty essential to summer, but gas will work just fine. Requirement: Soy-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe:** Grilled Soft Shelled Crab With Shrimp Mayo (Soy-Free)

**Ingredients:**

- **Shrimp Mayo:**
  - 2 tablespoons unsalted butter
  - 1 bay leaf
  - 1/2 teaspoon kosher salt
  - 1/2 teaspoon dry mustard
  - 1/2 teaspoon cayenne pepper
  - 1/4 teaspoon black pepper
  - 3 tablespoons shallot, finely chopped
  - 1/4 teaspoon dried basil
  - 1/8 teaspoon dried thyme
  - 1 tablespoon celery, finely chopped
  - 4 large shrimp, peeled
  - 1 egg
  - 1 1/4 cups extra virgin olive oil
  - 2 teaspoons lemon juice
  - 2 teaspoons apple cider vinegar
  
- **Grilled Soft Shelled Crab:**
  - 6 soft shelled crab
  - Salt and pepper to taste
  - 6 buns (ensure they are soy-free)
  - Arugula

**Instructions:**

1. In a small saucepan over medium heat, melt the butter.
2. Add bay leaf, salt, mustard, cayenne, black pepper, basil, and thyme. Heat until fragrant, about 1 minute.
3. Add shallot and celery, and sauté for 1 minute, stirring constantly.
4. Add shrimp, reduce heat to low, and cook for 5 minutes, stirring constantly.
5. Remove from heat and cool for about 15 minutes.
6. In a food processor or blender, process the egg for about 30 seconds. Add the shrimp mixture and blend for a few seconds more.
7. With the motor running, gradually add the olive oil in a steady stream to emulsify.
8. Stir in lemon juice and apple cider vinegar.
9. Thoroughly clean the soft shelled crab. Using kitchen shears, cut off the front of the crab, about 1/2 inch behind the eyes and mouth. Squeeze out the contents of the sack located directly behind the cut just made.
10. Season the crab with salt and pepper.
11. Prepare your grill (charcoal preferred for smokiness, but gas will work), and grill the crab for 2-3 minutes on each side.
12. Remove the crab from the grill and toast the buns. Put the crab on the bun and add a tablespoon of shrimp mayo and some arugula.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

**Requirement Fulfillment:**

- The modified recipe aims to be soy-free. However, it is crucial to ensure that all additional ingredients, especially the buns, are certifiably soy-free. Without explicit certification of soy-free status for such processed ingredients as buns, there is a potential risk of soy contamination.

- Additionally, it's advisable to verify that all other ingredients have not been exposed to cross-contamination with soy during production or processing.

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Spinach and Ricotta Pizza (Gluten-Free)**

**Ingredients:**
- Gluten-free cooking spray
- 1 tablespoon extra-virgin olive oil
- 2 tablespoons grated fresh Parmesan cheese
- 1 1/2 cups loosely packed baby spinach leaves
- 1 teaspoon minced garlic
- 1 1/4 cups (5 ounces) shredded part-skim mozzarella cheese
- 1/3 cup part-skim ricotta cheese
- 2 plum tomatoes, cored and thinly sliced
- Gluten-free pizza dough (check for gluten-free certification)

**Directions:**
1. Remove Gluten-Free Pizza Dough from refrigerator and let stand at room temperature for 1 hour.
2. Preheat oven to 500°F.
3. Coat a 12-inch perforated pizza pan with gluten-free cooking spray.
4. Place dough on a lightly floured (using gluten-free flour) surface. Roll into a 12-inch circle. Transfer dough to prepared pan, shaking off excess flour.
5. Brush dough evenly with olive oil. Spread gluten-free New York-Style Pizza Sauce evenly over dough, leaving a 1/4-inch border.
6. Sprinkle with Parmesan; top evenly with spinach and garlic.
7. Sprinkle mozzarella over spinach.
8. Spoon teaspoonfuls of ricotta over mozzarella.
9. Bake at 500°F for 12 minutes or until mozzarella melts and crust browns.
10. Let stand 5 minutes; top with tomato slices.
11. Cut into 6 wedges.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:

Let sit 15 a 30 minutes.", "", "Preheat the oven to 350A\u00b0. Toss the tofu, soy sauce, and sesame oil in bowl. Place the tofu in a single layer on a lined baking sheet. Requirement: Shellfish-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
### Modified Recipe: Thai Tofu Quinoa Bowls

#### Ingredients
- 1 cup uncooked quinoa
- 1 1/2 cups certified shellfish-free vegetable broth
- 1 package extra firm tofu (15 oz), diced
- 1 cup shredded carrots
- 2/3 cup chopped scallions
- 1/2 cup slivered almonds
- 1 tablespoon sesame seeds (optional)
- 1/2 cup fresh cilantro
- 2 tablespoons certified shellfish-free tamari or soy sauce
- 1 tablespoon toasted sesame oil
- 1/2 tablespoon vegetable oil
- 3 tablespoons certified shellfish-free sweet chili sauce
- 2 tablespoons rice wine vinegar
- 3 tablespoons coconut milk
- 1 teaspoon certified shellfish-free Sriracha
- 1/2 tablespoon brown sugar
- 2 teaspoons creamy peanut butter
- 1 garlic clove, minced
- 1/2 lime, juice
- 1 teaspoon grated ginger

#### Instructions
1. **Prepare Tofu:** Drain and rinse the block of tofu. Wrap it in a clean dish towel or paper towels, and place it on a rimmed dinner plate. Place another plate on top and weight it down with something heavy, like a can of tomatoes or a heavy skillet, to press out some of the excess liquid. Let sit for 15 to 30 minutes.

2. **Bake Tofu:** Preheat the oven to 350°F (175°C). Toss the tofu with tamari or soy sauce and toasted sesame oil in a bowl. Place the tofu in a single layer on a lined baking sheet. Bake for 35-40 minutes, tossing every ten minutes to crisp the tofu on all sides.

3. **Toast Quinoa:** Place a medium-sized saucepan on medium-low heat. Add in the dry quinoa and toast for 5 minutes, stirring occasionally, until golden brown and nutty in scent. Pour toasted quinoa into a fine mesh strainer and rinse thoroughly. Return to pot and add the vegetable broth. Lower heat slightly, cover, and cook for 12-15 minutes until all liquid is absorbed. Fluff quinoa with a fork once cooked, and set aside.

4. **Make Sauce:** Place the peanut butter in a bowl and microwave for 10 seconds to melt slightly. Add in the remaining sauce ingredients: sweet chili sauce, coconut milk, Sriracha, brown sugar, garlic, lime juice, and ginger. Whisk well to combine and set aside.

5. **Toast Almonds:** Place the almonds, sesame seeds, and vegetable oil in a small saucepan. Cook over medium-low heat, stirring occasionally, until the almonds are a deep golden brown.

6. **Combine:** Toss together the quinoa, carrots, scallions, cilantro, tofu, and 3/4 of the almond-sesame mixture. Pour over the sauce and toss well to combine.

7. **Serve:** Spoon into bowls and top with remaining nuts. Garnish with extra lime and Sriracha if desired. Can be stored in the fridge for up to one week.
```

Case 183-Title: Tabbouleh(A Middle Eastern Salad)  
Ingredients: ["1/2 c. fine burghul (cracked wheat)", "2 large tomatoes, diced", "1 bunch green onions, chopped", "4 bunches parsley, chopped", "1/2 bunch mint, chopped or 2 Tbsp. dried mint", "1 large cucumber, chopped", "1/2 c. olive oil", "juice of 3 lemons", "1 Tbsp. salt", "1/2 tsp. pepper"]
Directions: ["Rinse burghul well; drain and place in a large bowl.", "Add all chopped vegetables and mix well.", "Add oil, lemon juice, salt and pepper.", "Allow burghul mixture to set about 1 hour so juice will be absorbed by wheat.", "Serve on fresh green lettuce with Pita bread."]
Requirement: Dairy-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Dish Name:** Tabbouleh (Dairy-Free Version)  

**Ingredients:**
- 1/2 cup quinoa, rinsed and drained
- 2 large tomatoes, diced
- 1 bunch green onions, chopped
- 4 bunches parsley, chopped
- 1/2 bunch mint, chopped or 2 Tbsp dried mint
- 1 large cucumber, chopped
- 1/2 cup extra-virgin olive oil
- Juice of 3 lemons
- 1 Tbsp salt
- 1/2 tsp black pepper

**Directions:**
1. Cook the quinoa according to package instructions. Once cooked, allow it to cool completely.  
2. In a large bowl, combine the cooled quinoa, diced tomatoes, chopped green onions, parsley, mint, and cucumber. Mix well.
3. In a separate bowl, whisk together the olive oil, lemon juice, salt, and pepper.
4. Pour the dressing over the quinoa mixture and toss to coat evenly.
5. Allow the mixture to set for about 1 hour to let the flavors meld together.
6. Serve on fresh green lettuce with warm pita bread.
```

The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Black Bean Vegetable Salad**

**Ingredients:**
- 3 cups fresh or frozen corn
- 1 can (15 ounces) black beans, rinsed and drained
- 3 medium tomatoes, seeded and diced
- 1 cup chopped green pepper
- 1 cup chopped sweet red pepper
- 1/4 cup extra virgin olive oil
- 3 tablespoons freshly squeezed lime juice
- 2 tablespoons minced fresh cilantro
- 1 garlic clove, minced
- 1 teaspoon salt
- 1/2 teaspoon ground black pepper

**Directions:**
1. In a large bowl, combine the corn, black beans, tomatoes, green pepper, and sweet red pepper.
2. In a small bowl, whisk together the extra virgin olive oil, lime juice, minced cilantro, minced garlic, salt, and ground black pepper until well combined.
3. Pour the dressing over the vegetables; toss to coat evenly.
4. Cover and refrigerate for at least 2 hours before serving to allow the flavors to meld.
5. Serve chilled and enjoy your shellfish-free Black Bean Vegetable Salad.
```

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Baja Salmon Avocado**

**Ingredients:**
- 14 3/4 ounces wild-caught salmon, drained and flaked (skin and bones removed)
- 2 avocados, halved
- 1 tablespoon lemon juice
- 1 tablespoon lime juice
- 1 tablespoon chili powder (ensure it's mustard-free)
- 1 cup tomatoes, chopped
- 1 cup white onion, chopped
- 2 - 3 jalapenos, chopped
- 1/2 cup fresh cilantro, chopped

**Directions:**
1. Cut avocados in half and scoop out the flesh, leaving a 1/4 inch rim for the shell.
2. Set aside the halved avocado shells.
3. Dice the reserved avocado flesh and combine it with the remaining ingredients.
4. In a separate bowl, combine the flaked salmon, lemon juice, lime juice, and chili powder; stir gently.
5. Toss the diced avocado, tomatoes, onion, jalapeno, and cilantro with the seasoned salmon mixture until well combined.
6. Fill the avocado shells with the salmon and tomato mixture.
7. Serve with hot sauce (ensure it is mustard-free) and tortilla chips if desired.
```

The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe: Miniature Reubens (Peanut-Free)**

**Ingredients:**
- 8 ounces rye bread, cut into small pieces
- 1/4 cup mayonnaise (ensure peanut-free)
- 1 tablespoon tomato-based chili sauce (ensure peanut-free)
- 1/2 teaspoon prepared horseradish
- 1/2 small green bell pepper, minced
- 1/4 pound corned beef, thinly sliced
- 8 ounces sauerkraut, drained
- 8 ounces swiss cheese slices

**Directions:**
1. Preheat oven to 350°F (180°C).
2. Arrange bread slices on a large cookie sheet.
3. Bake for 5 minutes or until lightly browned on one side.
4. Remove cookie sheet from oven.
5. Meanwhile, in a small bowl, stir together mayonnaise, chili sauce, horseradish, and minced green bell pepper until blended.
6. With a knife, spread some mayonnaise mixture on the toasted side of each bread slice.
7. Top each slice with some corned beef, sauerkraut, and then swiss cheese, cutting corned beef and cheese slices to fit.
8. Bake for about 10 minutes or until cheese is melted.
9. Serve immediately.
```

```markdown
**Modified Chocolate Lush Recipe**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 1/2 c. gluten-free graham cracker crumbs (ensure peanut-free)
- 1/4 c. coconut sugar or granulated sugar
- 1/3 c. melted dairy-free butter substitute (such as coconut oil or soy margarine)
- 1 pkg. (8 oz.) dairy-free cream cheese, softened
- 1/4 c. coconut sugar or granulated sugar
- 2 tbsp. unsweetened almond milk or any other non-dairy milk
- 1 container (8 oz.) dairy-free whipped topping (ensure peanut-free)
- 2 packages (4 serving size each) dairy-free, gluten-free chocolate-flavored pudding mix (ensure peanut-free)
- 3 1/2 c. unsweetened almond milk or any other non-dairy milk

**Directions:**
1. Combine the gluten-free graham cracker crumbs, 1/4 c. coconut sugar, and melted dairy-free butter substitute in a bowl.
2. Press the mixture firmly into the bottom of a 13 x 9 inch pan to form a crust.
3. In another bowl, beat the dairy-free cream cheese with 1/4 c. coconut sugar and 2 Tbsp. of non-dairy milk until smooth.
4. Fold in half the container of dairy-free whipped topping into the cream cheese mixture.
5. Spread the cream cheese mixture evenly over the graham cracker crust.
6. Using 3 1/2 c. non-dairy milk, prepare the pudding according to the package directions.
7. Pour the prepared pudding over the cream cheese layer.
8. Refrigerate the dish for several hours or overnight until set.
9. Once set, spread the remaining dairy-free whipped topping over the pudding layer.
10. Garnish with grated dairy-free chocolate or chopped nuts, if desired, ensuring they are peanut-free.
11. Cut into servings and enjoy. Makes 12 to 15 servings.

Note: Ensure all packaged ingredients are checked for peanut allergens before use.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

```markdown
  - 1 cup bick's sliced beet (check for gluten-free certification)
  - 8 cups baby spinach, stemmed
  - 1/2 small red onion, sliced into rings
  - 2 pears, peeled and thinly sliced
  - 1/2 cup toasted sliced almonds (check for gluten-free certification)

5. Sprinkle with toasted sliced almonds just before serving.

```

```markdown
**Modified Bread Pudding Recipe (Dairy-Free)**

- 1 stick vegan butter (ensure dairy-free)
- 1 1/2 cups sugar
- 3 eggs
- 1 large can (12 oz) coconut milk
- 1 cup water
- 1 teaspoon vanilla extract
- Pinch of salt
- 2 to 3 loaves French bread, sliced
- Nutmeg, for sprinkling

**Instructions:**
1. Preheat the oven to 350°F (175°C).
2. In a mixing bowl, cream together the vegan butter and sugar until well combined.
3. Add the eggs, one at a time, beating well after each addition.
4. Stir in the coconut milk, water, vanilla extract, and salt until fully incorporated.
5. Pour the mixture into an 8x8-inch baking dish.
6. Break the French bread into pieces and place them into the liquid mixture, ensuring each piece is well-saturated, with the crust side facing up.
7. Sprinkle nutmeg evenly over the top.
8. Bake in the preheated oven for 30 minutes, or until the bread pudding has set and the top is lightly browned.
```

```markdown
**Ingredients:**
- 1/4 cup extra-virgin olive oil
- 1/2 lb. boneless skinless chicken breasts, chopped
- 1 can (14-1/2 oz.) stewed tomatoes, undrained
- 1 cup low-sodium chicken broth
- 1 zucchini, chopped
- 1/2 cup whole grain elbow macaroni, uncooked
- 1 tsp. dried basil leaves
- 1/2 cup dairy-free mozzarella cheese (ensure it's free from celery derivatives)

**Instructions:**
1. Heat olive oil in a large saucepan over medium heat.
2. Add chicken and cook for 3 minutes, stirring once.
3. Add tomatoes, broth, zucchini, macaroni, and basil to the saucepan.
4. Bring the mixture to a boil over high heat.
5. Reduce the heat to medium and simmer for 8 minutes, or until the macaroni is tender.
6. Sprinkle with dairy-free mozzarella cheese before serving.
```

Case 193-Title: Simple Stuffed Shells (With No Meat Option)
Ingredients: ["1 (12 ounce) box jumbo pasta shells, cooked and drained", "1 -2 cup light ricotta cheese (use full amount if not using meat or for extra cheesey)", "1 1/2 cups cooked sausage, crumbled (optional)", "1 cup part-skim mozzarella cheese, shredded, divided", "1/2 cup fresh parsley leaves, packed, very finely chopped", "1/4 cup fresh romano cheese or 1/4 cup parmesan cheese, grated", "1 large egg", "1 tablespoon finely minced garlic (optional) or 2 teaspoons garlic powder (optional)", "1/4 teaspoon nutmeg, grated", "1/8 teaspoon black pepper, to taste", "1 (26 ounce) jar marinara sauce or (26 ounce) jar homemade pasta sauce"]
Directions: ["Preheat oven to 375 F and grease a 9x13\" casserole; if you have not already done so, prepare pasta shells according to package directions and also brown your sausage, drain & crumble.", "Meanwhile, combine 1/2 cup of the mozzarella cheese, all of the ricotta (use 2 cups if not using meat or if you like it very cheesey, even if you are using meat, otherwise use just 1 cup), as well as the parsley (reserving a small amount to garnish), egg, Parmesan cheese, garlic, nutmeg and black pepper.", "Pour sauce into the baking dish and then set the unfilled shells on top facing up so that you can fill them.", "Evenly portion out the crumbled sausage, if using, in the bottom of each shell.", "Spoon filling to a large ziptop plastic bag and snip off one corner.", "Pipe about 2 Tbsp filling into the each of the prepared pasta shells, or as much or as little as you prefer.", "Cover with foil and bake for 30-35 minutes or until sauce is bubbling under the foil.", "Remove foil, sprinkle with the remaining 1/2 cup mozzarella cheese and bake, uncovered, for about 5 minutes or until the cheese melts.", "Serve extra sauce from the pan on the side."]
Requirement: Wheat-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Dish Name:** Gluten-Free Simple Stuffed Shells

**Ingredients:**
- 1 (12-ounce) box gluten-free jumbo pasta shells, cooked and drained
- 1-2 cups light ricotta cheese (use full amount if not using meat or for extra cheesey)
- 1 1/2 cups cooked sausage, crumbled (optional)
- 1 cup part-skim mozzarella cheese, shredded, divided
- 1/2 cup fresh parsley leaves, packed, very finely chopped
- 1/4 cup fresh romano cheese or 1/4 cup parmesan cheese, grated
- 1 large egg
- 1 tablespoon finely minced garlic (optional) or 2 teaspoons garlic powder (optional)
- 1/4 teaspoon nutmeg, grated
- 1/8 teaspoon black pepper, to taste
- 1 (26-ounce) jar gluten-free marinara sauce or (26-ounce) jar homemade pasta sauce

**Instructions:**
1. Preheat oven to 375°F and grease a 9x13" casserole dish. Prepare the gluten-free pasta shells according to package directions and, if using, brown the sausage, then drain and crumble it.
2. Meanwhile, in a mixing bowl, combine 1/2 cup of the mozzarella cheese, all of the ricotta (use 2 cups if not using meat or for extra cheesey, even if using meat, otherwise use just 1 cup), parsley (reserve a small amount to garnish), egg, Parmesan cheese, garlic, nutmeg, and black pepper.
3. Pour the gluten-free marinara sauce into the greased baking dish and then set the unfilled shells on top facing up so that you can fill them.
4. Evenly portion out the crumbled sausage, if using, into the bottom of each shell.
5. Spoon the cheese filling into a large zip-top plastic bag and snip off one corner to create a piping bag.
6. Pipe about 2 tablespoons of filling into each prepared pasta shell or adjust the amount according to preference.
7. Cover the casserole with foil and bake for 30-35 minutes or until the sauce is bubbling under the foil.
8. Remove the foil, sprinkle with the remaining 1/2 cup of mozzarella cheese, and bake uncovered for about 5 minutes or until the cheese melts.
9. Serve with extra sauce from the pan on the side.
```

Case 194-Title: G.F.G.S.
Ingredients: ["6 ounces butter, room temp", "1 cup sugar", "2 large eggs, room temp (or soak for 5 minutes in warm water)", "2 ounces molasses", "1/1/2 cups sweet white rice flour, toasted", "1/4 cup buckwheat flour", "1 teaspoon baking soda", "1 teaspoon cinnamon", "1 teaspoon ground ginger", "1/2 teaspoon sea or kosher salt", "1/4 teaspoon ground black pepper", "Zest of one lime"]
Directions: ["Preheat oven to 350 degrees. Line 2 baking sheets with parchment.", "Spread sweet white rice flour on one of the baking sheets. Place in oven and bake for 15-20 minutes until it is a pale brown - think of the color of a manilla folder. Remove and allow to cool while you gather the rest of your ingredients.", "Sift the dry ingredients onto a sheet of parchment. Yes, it's fine to use one that will eventually line one of your baking sheets.", "Using a stand mixer fitted with the paddle, cream together the butter and sugar until pale-colored and fluffy. Add molasses and mix well. With mixer running on low speed, add eggs one at a time, allowing each to be fully incorporated before adding the next. Stop mixer after the last one is added and scrape thoroughly all around the sides and bottom of the bowl. Raise bowl back up and mix again. Tip dry ingredients into the bowl. Also add the lime zest. Buckwheat flour consists of great, huge particles, so the batter needs to sit for about 15 minutes to let it fully hydrate. If you skip this step, the cookies will tend to have a raw sort of taste. You'll notice that the batter will be noticeably thicker after its nap.", "Use a small ice cream scoop or a teaspoon to drop the cookies. Leave about 2\" between them because they will spread. Requirement: Wheat-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Dish Name:** G.F.G.S. (Gluten-Free Ginger Spice Cookies)

**Ingredients:**
- 6 ounces plant-based margarine, room temp (ensure gluten-free)
- 1 cup coconut sugar
- 2 large eggs, room temp (or soak for 5 minutes in warm water)
- 2 ounces molasses
- 1 1/2 cups sweet white rice flour, toasted
- 1/4 cup sorghum flour
- 1 teaspoon baking soda
- 1 teaspoon cinnamon
- 1 teaspoon ground ginger
- 1/2 teaspoon sea or kosher salt
- 1/4 teaspoon ground black pepper
- Zest of one lime

**Instructions:**
1. Preheat oven to 350 degrees. Line 2 baking sheets with parchment.
2. Spread sweet white rice flour on one of the baking sheets. Place in the oven and bake for 15-20 minutes until it is a pale brown - think of the color of a manila folder. Remove and allow to cool while you gather the rest of your ingredients.
3. Sift the dry ingredients (toasted rice flour, sorghum flour, baking soda, cinnamon, ginger, salt, and pepper) onto a sheet of parchment. It's fine to use one that will eventually line one of your baking sheets.
4. Using a stand mixer fitted with the paddle, cream together the plant-based margarine and coconut sugar until pale-colored and fluffy. Add molasses and mix well. With mixer running on low speed, add eggs one at a time, allowing each to be fully incorporated before adding the next. Stop mixer after the last one is added and scrape thoroughly all around the sides and bottom of the bowl. Raise bowl back up and mix again.
5. Tip in the dry ingredients to the bowl. Also add the lime zest. Mix on low speed until all dry ingredients are incorporated. Scrape bowl and mix one last time.
6. Remove mixer bowl and cover with plastic. Let the batter sit for about 15 minutes to let the flours fully hydrate. The batter will be noticeably thicker after resting.
7. Use a small ice cream scoop or a teaspoon to drop the cookies. Leave about 2 inches between them because they will spread. Bake for 12-15 minutes, until very nicely browned and firm to the tap of a fingertip. Remove from oven and cool on a rack. Cookies will dry and crisp up as they cool.
8. Enjoy these cookies dunked in a cup of jasmine tea.
```

Add the onion and saute until translucent.", "3 Add the tomatoes and simmer with the onion until a thick sauce.", "4. Add the potatoes, garbanzo beans, turmeric, red pepper, coriander, and garam masala.
```markdown
**Modified Recipe for Aloo Chole**

**Ingredients:**
- 1 tablespoon oil (e.g., avocado oil, specifically labeled peanut-free)
- 1 teaspoon mustard seeds (ensure peanut-free certification)
- 1 teaspoon cumin seeds (ensure peanut-free certification)
- 1 medium white/yellow onion, finely chopped
- 1 large tomato (or approximately 10 cherry tomatoes), chopped
- 3 medium Yukon gold potatoes, peeled and diced
- 1 can (15 oz) garbanzo beans, drained and rinsed
- 1/2 teaspoon turmeric (ensure peanut-free certification)
- 1 teaspoon ground Aleppo pepper or paprika (ensure peanut-free certification)
- 1 teaspoon coriander powder (ensure peanut-free certification)
- 1 teaspoon garam masala (ensure peanut-free certification)

**Instructions:**
1. Ensure all ingredients are sourced from brands that are certified peanut-free.
2. Heat the peanut-free oil in a heavy pan or wok over medium heat.
3. Add the mustard seeds and cumin seeds, and toast until they begin to pop.
4. Add the chopped onion and sauté until translucent.
5. Stir in the tomatoes and cook down until they form a thick sauce.
6. Add the diced potatoes, garbanzo beans, turmeric, Aleppo pepper, coriander, and garam masala to the pan.
7. Cover the pan and reduce the heat to low. Allow the vegetables to steam in the sauce until they are tender, about 20 minutes.
8. Check the tenderness of the potatoes. Once done, adjust seasoning if necessary and serve hot.
```

Case 196-Title: Apricot And Pecan-Stuffed Pork Loin Roast
Ingredients: ["1 cup dried apricot", "1/2 cup chopped dried dates", "1/2 cup pecans", "1 clove garlic", "3/4 teaspoon salt (divided use)", "1/4 teaspoon fresh ground pepper", "4 tablespoons freshly chopped thyme (divided use)", "4 tablespoons molasses (divided use)", "4 tablespoons peanut oil or 4 tablespoons vegetable oil (divided use)", "5 lbs boneless pork loin roast, halved", "1 cup Bourbon", "1 cup chicken broth", "1/4 cup heavy whipping cream"]
Directions: ["Preheat oven to 350 degrees F.", "Coarsely chop apricots, dates, pecans, garlic, 1/2 teaspoon salt and pepper in a food processor.", "Add 2 tablespoons thyme, 1 tablespoon molasses and 2 tablespoons oil.", "Process until mixture is finely chopped, but not smooth.", "To butterfly the roast, make a lengthwise cut down the center of each roast half, cutting to, but not through, the bottom.", "Starting from the cut that was just made, slice horizontally toward one side, stopping 1/2 inch from edge.", "Repeat with other roast half.", "Open each half and flatten to a 1/2-inch thickness using a meat mallet or rolling pin.", "Spread apricot mixture evenly over pork.", "Roll each half, jellyroll fashion, starting with long side.", "Secure with string.", "Place both rolls, seam side down, in a shallow roasting pan.", "Brush with remaining 2 tablespoons oil and sprinkle with remaining thyme.", "Bring bourbon, broth and remaining 3 tablespoons molasses to a boil in a large saucepan.", "Remove from heat.", "Carefully ignite bourbon mixture with a long match.", "When flames die, pour over rolls.", "Bake 1 to 11/2 hours, or until meat thermometer inserted in thickest portion registers 160 F.", "Remove pork from pan and keep warm; reserve drippings.", "Pour reserved drippings in a small saucepan.", "Add cream and remaining salt.", "Cook over medium-high heat, stirring constantly, until slightly thickened.", "Slice pork and serve with sauce."]
Requirement: Celery-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
### Modified Recipe: Apricot and Pecan-Stuffed Pork Loin Roast

#### Ingredients
- 1 cup dried apricot
- 1/2 cup chopped dried dates
- 1/2 cup pecans
- 1 clove garlic
- 3/4 teaspoon salt (divided use)
- 1/4 teaspoon fresh ground pepper
- 4 tablespoons freshly chopped thyme (divided use)
- 4 tablespoons molasses (divided use)
- 4 tablespoons sunflower oil (divided use)
- 5 lbs boneless pork loin roast, halved
- 1 cup Bourbon
- 1 cup unsalted chicken broth
- 1/4 cup coconut cream

#### Directions
1. Preheat oven to 350 degrees F.
2. Coarsely chop apricots, dates, pecans, garlic, 1/2 teaspoon salt, and pepper in a food processor.
3. Add 2 tablespoons thyme, 1 tablespoon molasses, and 2 tablespoons oil.
4. Process until the mixture is finely chopped, but not smooth.
5. To butterfly the roast, make a lengthwise cut down the center of each roast half, cutting to, but not through, the bottom.
6. Starting from the cut that was just made, slice horizontally toward one side, stopping 1/2 inch from the edge.
7. Repeat with the other roast half.
8. Open each half and flatten to a 1/2-inch thickness using a meat mallet or rolling pin.
9. Spread apricot mixture evenly over pork.
10. Roll each half, jellyroll fashion, starting with long side.
11. Secure with string.
12. Place both rolls, seam side down, in a shallow roasting pan.
13. Brush with remaining 2 tablespoons oil and sprinkle with remaining thyme.
14. Bring bourbon, broth, and remaining 3 tablespoons molasses to a boil in a large saucepan.
15. Remove from heat.
16. Carefully ignite bourbon mixture with a long match.
17. When flames die, pour over rolls.
18. Bake 1 to 1 1/2 hours, or until a meat thermometer inserted in the thickest portion registers 160 F.
19. Remove pork from pan and keep warm; reserve drippings.
20. Pour reserved drippings into a small saucepan.
21. Add coconut cream and remaining salt.
22. Cook over medium-high heat, stirring constantly, until slightly thickened.
23. Slice pork and serve with sauce.
```

Case 197-Title: Nigella Lawson'S No-Bake Nutella Cheesecake
Ingredients: ["250 grams digestive biscuits (one 8.8-ounce package), or substitute graham crackers or chocolate wafer cookies", "75 grams (5 tablespoons plus 1 teaspoon) soft unsalted butter", "400 grams (one 371-gram jar is fine) Nutella, at room temperature, divided", "100 grams (2/3 cup) hazelnuts, well-toasted and chopped (see note), divided", "500 grams (two 8-ounce packages is fine) cream cheese, at room temperature", "60 grams (1/2 cup) confectioners' sugar, sifted"]
Directions: ["Break the digestives into the bowl of a processor, add the butter and a 15-milliliter tablespoon of Nutella, and blitz until it starts to clump. Add 25 grams/3 tablespoons of the hazelnuts and continue to pulse until you have a damp, sandy mixture.", "Tip into a 23-centimeter/9-inch round springform and press into the base either using your hands or the back of a spoon. Place in the fridge to chill.", "Beat the cream cheese and confectioners' sugar until smooth and then add the remaining Nutella to the cream cheese mixture, and continue beating until combined.", "Take the springform out of the fridge and carefully smooth the Nutella mixture over the base. Scatter the remaining chopped hazelnuts on top to cover and place the tin in the fridge for at least four hours or overnight. Serve straight from the fridge for best results.", "Editor's note: I like to toast nuts on a rimmed baking sheet at 325\u00b0 F for 15 to 20 minutes, until they are golden through the middle. To keep this truly no-bake, you can also toast the nuts in a dry pan on the stovetop over medium low, tossing occasionally. To get any loose skins off, leave them to cool and steam a bit wrapped in a clean kitchen towel for 10 minutes, then rub off as much skin as you can before chopping."]
Requirement: Sulfite-free

Result:
The newly generated recipe is:

```markdown
**Modified Recipe for Sulfite-Free No-Bake Nutella Cheesecake**

**Ingredients:**

- 250 grams digestive biscuits (ensure sulfite-free) or substitute with sulfite-free graham crackers or chocolate wafer cookies
- 75 grams (5 tablespoons plus 1 teaspoon) soft unsalted butter (ensure sulfite-free)
- 400 grams (one 371-gram jar is fine) Nutella, at room temperature, divided (check for sulfite-free option)
- 100 grams (2/3 cup) hazelnuts, well-toasted and chopped, divided
- 500 grams (two 8-ounce packages is fine) cream cheese, at room temperature
- 60 grams (1/2 cup) confectioners' sugar, sifted (ensure sulfite-free)

**Directions:**

1. Break the digestive biscuits or cookies into the bowl of a processor, add the butter and a 15-milliliter tablespoon of Nutella, and blitz until it starts to clump. Add 25 grams/3 tablespoons of the hazelnuts and continue to pulse until you have a damp, sandy mixture.

2. Tip into a 23-centimeter/9-inch round springform and press into the base using your hands or the back of a spoon. Place in the fridge to chill.

3. Beat the cream cheese and confectioners' sugar until smooth and then add the remaining Nutella to the cream cheese mixture, and continue beating until combined.

4. Take the springform out of the fridge and carefully smooth the Nutella mixture over the base. Scatter the remaining chopped hazelnuts on top to cover and place the tin in the fridge for at least four hours or overnight. Serve straight from the fridge for best results.

5. To toast the hazelnuts (optional): Place them in a dry pan on the stovetop over medium-low, tossing occasionally until golden through the middle. Let them cool wrapped in a clean kitchen towel for 10 minutes, then rub off as much skin as you can before chopping.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

Ensure all modified ingredients are explicitly certified sulfite-free. Digestive biscuits, graham crackers, chocolate wafer cookies, unsalted butter, Nutella, and confectioners' sugar are all ingredients that potentially contain sulfites either as preservatives or through cross-contamination during processing. Obtain products that are labeled sulfite-free to meet the requirement.

Check Nutella for sulfite content. Nutella, as a mass-produced spread, might include ingredients with natural sulfites or added preservatives. Verify the absence of sulfites in the specific brand to avoid ingestion risks for individuals sensitive to sulfites.

```markdown
**Modified Peppernut Tea Bread Recipe**

**Ingredients:** 
- 1 1/2 cups all-purpose flour
- 1 teaspoon baking soda
- 3/4 teaspoon salt
- 1/2 teaspoon grated whole nutmeg
- 1/2 teaspoon ground cinnamon
- 1/4 teaspoon ground star anise
- 1/4 teaspoon freshly ground black pepper
- 1 cup apple butter (ensure it's mustard-free)
- 1/4 cup sugar
- 1/4 cup honey (ensure it's mustard-free)
- 2 large eggs, lightly beaten
- 1/2 cup golden raisins
- 2 tablespoons sliced almonds, divided
- Cooking spray (ensure it's mustard-free)

**Directions:**
1. Preheat oven to 325°F.
2. Lightly spoon flour into dry measuring cups; level with a knife. Combine flour, baking soda, salt, nutmeg, cinnamon, star anise, and black pepper in a large bowl, stirring with a whisk.
3. Add apple butter, sugar, honey, and eggs to the flour mixture; stir with a whisk until well combined. Fold in raisins and 1 tablespoon almonds.
4. Spoon batter into a 9 x 5-inch loaf pan coated with cooking spray. Sprinkle with 1 tablespoon of almonds.
5. Bake at 325°F for 35 minutes or until a wooden pick inserted in center comes out clean. Loosen bread from sides of pan using a narrow metal spatula; turn out onto a wire rack; cool.
```

Evaluation of the recipe:
Caution

Requirement Fulfillment: The modified recipe specifies mustard-free apple butter, honey, and cooking spray. However, more clarity is needed:

- Potential Cross-Contamination: Without explicit information on all ingredients being processed in mustard-free facilities or explicitly certified mustard-free, especially concerning almonds and other ingredients, there remains a risk of cross-contamination.

For individuals with severe mustard allergies, it's crucial to verify each ingredient, especially packaged ones, for any mustard cross-contamination or presence.
